		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Also known as</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><ul><li>Half-Blood Prince<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[4]</a></sup></li><li>Snivellus<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[5]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[6]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DH33_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-6">[7]</a></sup> (by <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a>)</li><li>Sev<sup id="cite_ref-DH33_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-6">[7]</a></sup> (by <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a>)</li><li>Slytherus<sup id="cite_ref-PW_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PW-7">[8]</a></sup> (<i><a href="/wiki/Potterwatch" title="Potterwatch">Potterwatch</a></i>)  </li><li>The Potions master</li></ul></div>
</div>

</aside>

<div style="display:none;"></div>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>The <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a> are many, varied, ever-changing, and eternal. Fighting them is like fighting a many-headed monster, which, each time a neck is severed, sprouts a head even fiercer and cleverer than before. You are fighting that which is unfixed, mutating, indestructible.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Snape teaching <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<p><b>Severus Snape</b> (<a href="/wiki/9_January" title="9 January">9 January</a>, <a href="/wiki/1960" title="1960">1960</a><sup id="cite_ref-birth_0-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-birth-0">[1]</a></sup> – <a href="/wiki/2_May" title="2 May">2 May</a>, <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a><sup id="cite_ref-death_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-death-1">[2]</a></sup>) was an <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">English</a> <a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">half-blood</a><sup id="cite_ref-blood_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-blood-2">[3]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> serving as <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a> <span class="template-c">(1981-1996)</span>, <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">professor</a> <span class="template-c">(1996-1997)</span>, and <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> <span class="template-c">(1997-1998)</span> of the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> as well as a member of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a>. His double life played an extremely important role in both of the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_Wars" title="Wizarding Wars">Wizarding Wars</a> against <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>. The only child of <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> <a href="/wiki/Tobias_Snape" title="Tobias Snape">Tobias Snape</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gobstones" title="Gobstones">Gobstones</a> witch <a href="/wiki/Eileen_Prince" title="Eileen Prince">Eileen Snape</a> <span class="template-c">(née <a href="/wiki/Prince_family" title="Prince family">Prince</a>)</span>, Severus was raised in the <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> dwelling of <a href="/wiki/Spinner%27s_End" title="Spinner's End">Spinner's End</a>, which was in close proximity to the home of the <a href="/wiki/Evans_family" title="Evans family">Evans family</a>, though in a poorer area. He met <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily</a> and <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Petunia Evans</a> when he was nine and fell deeply in <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a> with Lily, becoming a close friend of hers. 
</p><p>Severus started at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> with Lily in <a href="/wiki/1971" title="1971">1971</a>, where he was Sorted into <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin House</a>. This put him in the same year as Lily but unfortunately for him in rival houses. Severus became the immediate enemy of <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> and was a frequent victim of their bullying. This led him to be irritable towards James's son Harry when he was a professor. Snape, when young, developed a passion for the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a>, which increased as his desire for revenge grew stronger. Snape became involved with the bullies in <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin House</a>, many of whom were <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood_supremacy" title="Pure-blood supremacy">pure-blood supremacists</a>. This put his friendship with Lily, a <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a>, under great strain until it was eventually broken in their fifth year. In an attempt to win back Lily's affections,<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[14]</a></sup> Snape joined the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> along with a group of his fellow Slytherins.
</p><p>Severus was made a member of the <a href="/wiki/Slug_Club" title="Slug Club">Slug Club</a> presumably because of his talent in <a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">Potion-making</a> and <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a> kept a picture of him as a student, clutching <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_copy_of_Advanced_Potion-Making" title="Severus Snape's copy of Advanced Potion-Making">his copy</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Advanced_Potion-Making" title="Advanced Potion-Making">Advanced Potion-Making</a></i>. Despite this, Horace did not have many hopes for Severus's future, as his photograph was kept behind many others.<sup id="cite_ref-script_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-script-14">[15]</a></sup>
</p><p>Shortly before Lily Evans was murdered by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, Snape changed sides and became a member of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> as well as a double agent during the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>. With tremendous difficulty, Snape prevented Lord Voldemort from learning the truth about his loyalties. Despite the opinions of most others including <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> during his early life, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> trusted Snape for reasons that were kept between them both until their deaths. Despite Snape killing Dumbledore, it is learned that they had a special agreement for him to do so. When he died, it was revealed that his deep strong love for <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> caused him to redeem himself, joining Dumbledore's cause for her protection (and, after her death, that of her son) from Lord Voldemort.
</p><p>The relationship between Dumbledore and Snape would be one of an unusually strong loyalty, so much so that Snape agreed to kill Dumbledore upon the latter's own request. Before Dumbledore's death, Snape promised to protect the students of Hogwarts from the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, who would inevitably take control of the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> as well as the school. Snape later participated in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> but was murdered by Lord Voldemort who mistakenly believed that Snape was the master of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a> (an immensely strong and powerful wand that Voldemort deeply desired, as well as one of the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>) when in reality, Harry Potter was the master of the Elder Wand, because <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> had disarmed Dumbledore on the night of Dumbledore's death on top of the <a href="/wiki/Astronomy_Tower" title="Astronomy Tower">Astronomy Tower</a>, and Harry had disarmed <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco</a> at Malfoy Manor. 
</p><p>After Snape's death, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> ensured that his portrait remained at Hogwarts, honouring him as a hero, despite their significant personal differences. In addition, Harry later named his second son <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus Potter</a> in honour of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> and Severus, both of whom were an inspiration in Harry's life after the Battle of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. Harry also was influenced by Severus' Hogwarts house, and freely admitted that his son Albus could choose <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> if he wished.
</p>
<nav id="toc" class="toc" data-loaded="false"><div id="toctitle"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctoggle">[<a href="#" class="internal" id="togglelink" data-show="show" data-hide="hide">show</a>]</span></div><ol></ol></nav>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">Biography</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life_.281960-1971.29">Early life <span class="template-c">(1960-1971)</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Lily Evans</b>: "<i>Doesn’t your dad like magic?</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>He doesn’t like anything, much.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; Discussion of Snape's family and home life<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div><figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 208px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b7/Cokeworth.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161206210615" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Cokeworth"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Cokeworth.jpg" 	data-image-name="Cokeworth.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b7/Cokeworth.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/208?cb=20161206210615"  	 width="208"  	 height="155"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b7/Cokeworth.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/208?cb=20161206210615" 	 alt="Cokeworth"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Cokeworth.jpg" 	data-image-name="Cokeworth.jpg" 	 	 width="208"  	 height="155"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Cokeworth.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 	</figcaption> </figure>Severus Snape was born <a href="/wiki/9_January" title="9 January">9 January</a>, <a href="/wiki/1960" title="1960">1960</a> to <a href="/wiki/Eileen_Prince" title="Eileen Prince">Eileen Prince</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a> <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witch</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-15">[16]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Tobias_Snape" title="Tobias Snape">Tobias Snape</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-15">[16]</a></sup> making him a half-blood wizard. Severus, whose father was neglectful and possibly even violent, began to identify with his mother's family and created a secret nickname from his mother's maiden name, calling himself the "Half-Blood Prince". His unhappy relationship with his father may have been the origin of his disdain for Muggles. It is implied that Severus was friendless and uncared for by his parents. This lack of care largely shaped Severus's bitter disposition and cruel behaviour later in his life.
<p>Severus grew up at <a href="/wiki/Spinner%27s_End" title="Spinner's End">Spinner's End</a>, a shabby suburb of <a href="/wiki/Cokeworth" title="Cokeworth">Cokeworth</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermore_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermore-16">[17]</a></sup> This area of town was near a dirty river and full of dilapidated houses, disused factories and broken down street lamps. Through the rest of his life, Severus continued to return there when he was not at school. The young Severus is depicted as being unwashed and wearing ill-fitting clothes "<i>that were so mismatched that it looked deliberate</i>". As a child, Severus was neglected and his parents often fought with one another. He could not wait to leave for Hogwarts at the end of the summer.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 235px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c0/WB_F8_Lily_Severus_looking_at_each_other_young_flashback_HPDH2-07931.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161206062002" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="WB F8 Lily Severus looking at each other young flashback HPDH2-07931"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="WB_F8_Lily_Severus_looking_at_each_other_young_flashback_HPDH2-07931.jpg" 	data-image-name="WB F8 Lily Severus looking at each other young flashback HPDH2-07931.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c0/WB_F8_Lily_Severus_looking_at_each_other_young_flashback_HPDH2-07931.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20161206062002"  	 width="235"  	 height="157"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c0/WB_F8_Lily_Severus_looking_at_each_other_young_flashback_HPDH2-07931.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20161206062002" 	 alt="WB F8 Lily Severus looking at each other young flashback HPDH2-07931"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="WB_F8_Lily_Severus_looking_at_each_other_young_flashback_HPDH2-07931.jpg" 	data-image-name="WB F8 Lily Severus looking at each other young flashback HPDH2-07931.jpg" 	 	 width="235"  	 height="157"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:WB_F8_Lily_Severus_looking_at_each_other_young_flashback_HPDH2-07931.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape telling Lily that she is a witch</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> and her family lived in the same town, close to <a href="/wiki/Spinner%27s_End" title="Spinner's End">Spinner's End</a>. After watching her for some time, Severus noticed her evident magical abilities and began making friendly overtures. The two bonded quickly and it appears that he was very interested in Lily right from the beginning, though she only regarded him as a good friend. During this time he also developed a contempt towards her older sister, <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Petunia</a>. This was most likely because she made disparaging comments about his clothes and residence but may also be because she was a Muggle.
</p><p>Information from Severus's own memories of his first interactions with Lily and Petunia suggests that he was an awkward child with poor social skills. Even when it was important to him to make a good impression, he always seemed to have trouble doing so.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_years_.281971-1978.29">Hogwarts years <span class="template-c">(1971-1978)</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>James Potter</b>: "'<i>Gryffindor, where dwell the brave at heart!' Like my dad. Got a problem with that?</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>No. If you'd rather be brawny instead of brainy —</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Sirius Black</b>: "<i>Where are you hoping to go, seeing as you're neither?</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James</a>, Snape, and Sirius have an unpleasant first meeting<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div><figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 245px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0a/Harry-potter7-snape-sorting.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170912184017" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Harry-potter7-snape-sorting"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Harry-potter7-snape-sorting.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry-potter7-snape-sorting.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0a/Harry-potter7-snape-sorting.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170912184017"  	 width="245"  	 height="109"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0a/Harry-potter7-snape-sorting.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170912184017" 	 alt="Harry-potter7-snape-sorting"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Harry-potter7-snape-sorting.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry-potter7-snape-sorting.jpg" 	 	 width="245"  	 height="109"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter7-snape-sorting.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape shortly before being Sorted into <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Severus attended <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> as a student from <a href="/wiki/1971" title="1971">1971</a>-<a href="/wiki/1978" title="1978">1978</a> and was Sorted into <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin House</a>, at that time led by <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions master</a> <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>. On the way to Hogwarts for his first year, Severus sat with Lily Evans on the train. While on the train they met <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>. This encounter between the three of them revolved around a disagreement regarding what Hogwarts house was the best. This hostile first encounter would set the tone for the antagonism between the three of them for the rest of his life.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 245px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c7/Order-of-the-phoenix-teenage_Snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170501032542" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Order-of-the-phoenix-teenage Snape"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-teenage_Snape.jpg" 	data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-teenage Snape.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c7/Order-of-the-phoenix-teenage_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170501032542"  	 width="245"  	 height="113"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c7/Order-of-the-phoenix-teenage_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170501032542" 	 alt="Order-of-the-phoenix-teenage Snape"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-teenage_Snape.jpg" 	data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-teenage Snape.jpg" 	 	 width="245"  	 height="113"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order-of-the-phoenix-teenage_Snape.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape in his fifth year studying by the <a href="/wiki/Great_Lake" title="Great Lake">Black Lake</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sorted into Slytherin House upon their arrival at the school, classmates would later state that Severus excelled in the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a> from an early age. At the age of eleven, he knew more curses and hexes than most of the seventh year students. He was credited with creating a good number of popular spells like <i><a href="/wiki/Levicorpus" title="Levicorpus">Levicorpus</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Liberacorpus" title="Liberacorpus">Liberacorpus</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Muffliato_Charm" title="Muffliato Charm">Muffliato</a></i>, and curses like <i><a href="/wiki/Langlock" title="Langlock">Langlock</a></i>, the <a href="/wiki/Toenail-growing_hex" title="Toenail-growing hex">Toenail Growth Hex</a>, and his signature curse, <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i>. He reportedly was friends with a gang of Slytherins who later became <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, including <a href="/wiki/Avery_(Marauder-era)" title="Avery (Marauder-era)" class="mw-redirect">Avery</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mulciber_(Marauder-era)" title="Mulciber (Marauder-era)" class="mw-redirect">Mulciber</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Black</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rodolphus_Lestrange" title="Rodolphus Lestrange">Rodolphus Lestrange</a>, <a href="/wiki/Evan_Rosier" title="Evan Rosier">Evan Rosier</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wilkes" title="Wilkes">Wilkes</a>. Severus also had contact with <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>, who was a <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a> during his first year and greeted him kindly when he was Sorted into the Slytherin House. Most likely the two had good rapport at Hogwarts (which could also be a reason why <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa Malfoy</a> trusted Severus to take care of <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> and why he seemed to favour Draco during his later teaching years even when Draco refuses it in the task to kill Dumbledore).
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a> were also classmates of Severus. Around the same time, he also got acquainted with another notorious troublemaker; a <a href="/wiki/Fifth_year" title="Fifth year">Fifth year</a> student by the name of <a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</a> who not only was in the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">same house</a> as his new <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">school rivals</a>, but also actively sought to mentor her younger schoolmates in the art of mischief-making without getting caught: While popular with many of their peers for her, she was, on the other hand, strongly disliked by most of the teachers for her excessive rebellious streak, frequent rule-breaking and the bad influence she was on her younger housemates. No less discontent with her behaviour than their professors were, Severus's mistrust in Rakepick ran deeper still; she was an avid advocate for the existence of the fabled <a href="/wiki/Cursed_Vaults" title="Cursed Vaults">Cursed Vaults</a> of Hogwarts. While her claims were dismissed by the faculty of the day, young Snape, however, was not so certain; seeing her as uncommonly ambitious for a Gryffindor and, he recognised, far from stupid, he eventually came to question her motives and her intentions for the vaults, eventually coming to regard her as a danger to the school and all who resided at the castle.
</p><p>James and his group of friends were constantly at war with Severus throughout their school years. Severus's memories, recorded in the <a href="/wiki/Pensieve" title="Pensieve">Pensieve</a>, suggest that he was an introverted and studious individual, whereas James was arrogant, popular and athletic. Immediately upon meeting him, James disliked Severus for expressing a desire to be in Slytherin. James's big crush on Lily, and Severus's close friendship and unrequited love for her also heightened the tension between the two.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 239px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/James_tormenting_Severus_flashback.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140308030631" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="James tormenting Severus flashback"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="James_tormenting_Severus_flashback.gif" 	data-image-name="James tormenting Severus flashback.gif" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/James_tormenting_Severus_flashback.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/239?cb=20140308030631"  	 width="239"  	 height="128"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/James_tormenting_Severus_flashback.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/239?cb=20140308030631" 	 alt="James tormenting Severus flashback"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="James_tormenting_Severus_flashback.gif" 	data-image-name="James tormenting Severus flashback.gif" 	 	 width="239"  	 height="128"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:James_tormenting_Severus_flashback.gif" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape being bullied by the <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>One recorded memory in the Pensieve bears witness to James bullying him, turning him upside-down to reveal his underwear in front of many students, including Lily. Lily came to Severus's defence, but this only made things worse: in a subsequent lashing out at James in an attempt to recover his lost dignity, Severus inadvertently called Lily a <a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a>. Lily refused to forgive him for it, even after his repeated apologies. This would forever be Severus's <i>worst memory</i>
</p><p>Severus noticed that Remus kept disappearing during the full moon and once followed him past the <a href="/wiki/Whomping_Willow" title="Whomping Willow">Whomping Willow</a> (after being tipped off on how to do so by <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>) to confirm his suspicions. This act could have cost Severus his life or his humanity (he could have been turned into a werewolf by Remus's bite) if it had not been for James. When James found out what had happened, he went after Severus and managed to save him just before he got to the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a> while Remus was in his wolf-form. <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> swore Severus to secrecy, but the true nature of Remus was clear to Severus. By their seventh year, James had grown out of his immaturity and arrogance to the point that Lily agreed to start dating him, even though he never grew out of his hatred for Severus — according to Sirius, Severus had always been a "special case" with James. Lily ended up marrying James, which only strengthened Severus's bitterness towards him.
</p><p>There was also some overlap between his school career and that of a younger student by the name of <a href="/wiki/Jacob_(Hogwarts_student)" title="Jacob (Hogwarts student)">Jacob</a>, yet another rule-breaker Snape came to severely dislike. During the later part of his magical education, the school was plagued by several dangerous curses unleashed upon the school by Jacob after he tampered with the fabled <a href="/wiki/Cursed_Vaults" title="Cursed Vaults">Cursed Vaults</a>, which resulted in the death and injury of several of his peers, although he suffered no permanent injury himself.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Half-Blood_Prince">Half-Blood Prince</span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">"<i>This book is property of the Half-Blood Prince.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;The inside cover of the textbook<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>Severus was a talented wizard even in his childhood. It was apparent through the notes and scribbles in <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_copy_of_Advanced_Potion-Making" title="Severus Snape's copy of Advanced Potion-Making">his potions textbook</a> that he made time during classes to invent <a href="/wiki/Curse" title="Curse">curses</a>, <a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">charms</a>, and clever <a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">potion</a> innovations, while simultaneously learning the required textbook lessons.
</dd></dl>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 231px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Advanced_Potion_Making_pages.png/revision/latest?cb=20150115071854" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Advanced Potion Making pages"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Advanced_Potion_Making_pages.png" 	data-image-name="Advanced Potion Making pages.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Advanced_Potion_Making_pages.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/231?cb=20150115071854"  	 width="231"  	 height="174"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Advanced_Potion_Making_pages.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/231?cb=20150115071854" 	 alt="Advanced Potion Making pages"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Advanced_Potion_Making_pages.png" 	data-image-name="Advanced Potion Making pages.png" 	 	 width="231"  	 height="174"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Advanced_Potion_Making_pages.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Half-Blood Prince's many annotations and corrections</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Severus's potions textbook contained a few spells and curses which he was credited with inventing: <i><a href="/wiki/Levicorpus" title="Levicorpus">Levicorpus</a></i>, which grabbed the victim by the ankle and dangled him/her upside-down, and <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i>, which caused slashing bloody cuts (guided by the wand gestures of the caster, like a blade/sword) which bled extensively. <i>Levicorpus</i> somehow escaped from Severus's secrecy, and became very popular around Hogwarts towards the end of his fifth year at school. Some other spells included <i><a href="/wiki/Muffliato_Charm" title="Muffliato Charm">Muffliato</a></i>, which filled the ears of anyone nearby with an unidentifiable buzzing sound and <a href="/wiki/Toenail-growing_hex" title="Toenail-growing hex">another hex</a> that caused toenails to grow at an unnaturally fast rate. Severus's book later fell into the hands of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> in September 1996. Harry used the Half-Blood Prince's tips and earned praise with that year's Potions master, <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Professor Slughorn</a>. Harry considered the Half-Blood Prince to be a better teacher than Severus, unaware at that point that Severus <i>was</i> the Prince, much to Harry's later displeasure.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 251px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b1/Property_of_the_Half-Blood_Prince.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120729064810" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Property of the Half-Blood Prince"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Property_of_the_Half-Blood_Prince.jpg" 	data-image-name="Property of the Half-Blood Prince.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b1/Property_of_the_Half-Blood_Prince.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20120729064810"  	 width="251"  	 height="105"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b1/Property_of_the_Half-Blood_Prince.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20120729064810" 	 alt="Property of the Half-Blood Prince"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Property_of_the_Half-Blood_Prince.jpg" 	data-image-name="Property of the Half-Blood Prince.jpg" 	 	 width="251"  	 height="105"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Property_of_the_Half-Blood_Prince.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The inscription inside Snape's copy of Advanced Potion-Making</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">potions</a> textbook has an inscription indicating it is <i>Property of the Half-Blood Prince</i>. <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>'s research revealed that Prince was the maiden name of Severus's mother and so the nickname was revealed to be a combination of his mother's maiden name and his blood status. Harry Potter also pointed out the similarities between Snape's nickname and the name Voldemort gave himself. This nickname was apparently a secret, as <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus</a> did not remember it ever being used publicly by Severus.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="First_Wizarding_War_.281978-1981.29">First Wizarding War <span class="template-c">(1978-1981)</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="As_a_Death_Eater">As a Death Eater</span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>The one with the power to vanquish the Dark Lord approaches… Born to those who have thrice defied him, born as the seventh month dies….</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;The part of <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney's first prophecy">Sybill Trelawney's first prophecy</a> that Snape overheard<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div><figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 238px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/57/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-9207.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150723173722" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-9207"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-9207.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-9207.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/57/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-9207.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/238?cb=20150723173722"  	 width="238"  	 height="140"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/57/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-9207.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/238?cb=20150723173722" 	 alt="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-9207"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-9207.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-9207.jpg" 	 	 width="238"  	 height="140"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-9207.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape during his time as one of Lord Voldemort's Death Eaters</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
</dd></dl>
<p>Severus Snape eventually joined the ranks of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. His actions as a Death Eater are largely unknown, though he quickly became an important Death Eater in Voldemort's inner circle. He was the spy responsible for informing Voldemort about the prophecy foretelling his downfall. In early <a href="/wiki/1980" title="1980">1980</a>, Snape eavesdropped on an interview for <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a> Professor <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a> and <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head" title="Hog's Head" class="mw-redirect">Hog's Head Inn</a>. In the course of the interview, Trelawney prophesied that at the end of July, a child would be born who would cause the destruction of Lord Voldemort (which prompted Dumbledore to hire her, partly for her own safety). At that time it was not clear who was meant by the prophecy. Two children of prominent wizarding families were born that year at the end of July: <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>.
</p><p>Albus reported at the <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a> trial of <a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</a> that Severus had come to him and explained that he had been the one to overhear the prophecy, and reported it to Voldemort. However, Snape did not hear the entire prophecy, as the Hog's Head's barman and Albus' brother, <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth</a>, caught him eavesdropping and threw him out.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="As_a_double_agent">As a double agent</span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>If you loved <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a>, if you truly loved her, then your way forward is clear. You know how and why she died. Make sure it was not in vain. Help me protect Lily's son.</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>Very well. But never — never tell, Dumbledore! This must be between us! Swear it! I cannot bear... especially Potter's son...</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; Snape promises to protect Harry after Lily's murder<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div><figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/Snapegodricshollow.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110917012804" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Snapegodricshollow"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Snapegodricshollow.jpg" 	data-image-name="Snapegodricshollow.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/Snapegodricshollow.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110917012804"  	 width="180"  	 height="121"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/Snapegodricshollow.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110917012804" 	 alt="Snapegodricshollow"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Snapegodricshollow.jpg" 	data-image-name="Snapegodricshollow.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="121"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snapegodricshollow.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape next to Lily's House</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>Severus suffered terrible remorse when <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> decided that Harry Potter was the subject of the prophecy and that <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a>, the woman whom he always loved, was now in danger as a result of his actions. He begged Voldemort to spare her, who agreed. However, knowing that he could not leave Lily's safety in the hands of someone who could turn back at his word on a mere whim and that Lily would probably defend her child to the last breath, Snape also approached <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> to ask him to save Lily. He pleaded with Dumbledore to hide her, along with her husband and son if he had to. Dumbledore agreed but insisted that Severus serve him as a spy among the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. In fact, it was Snape's request to Voldemort which allowed Lily to let herself die in order for Harry to live when Voldemort attempted to murder him, his curse backfired and Voldemort's body was destroyed.
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/db/Severus_Snape_casting_a_Patronus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190228232400" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Severus Snape casting a Patronus"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Severus_Snape_casting_a_Patronus.gif" 	data-image-name="Severus Snape casting a Patronus.gif" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/db/Severus_Snape_casting_a_Patronus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190228232400"  	 width="180"  	 height="111"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/db/Severus_Snape_casting_a_Patronus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190228232400" 	 alt="Severus Snape casting a Patronus"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Severus_Snape_casting_a_Patronus.gif" 	data-image-name="Severus Snape casting a Patronus.gif" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="111"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Severus_Snape_casting_a_Patronus.gif" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape showing his love for Lily Evans, even after her death</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Despite Dumbledore's best efforts to protect the Potters, Voldemort was tipped off by <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, one of <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James</a>' best friends, a spy, and he found them anyway. After Lily's death, Snape was devastated and distraught to the point of wishing himself dead, but Dumbledore urged him to ensure Harry's safety out of respect for Lily's memory; Snape initially insisted the danger had been averted with the Dark Lord gone, only for Albus to insist that he would return and everyone, particularly the boy, would be in danger when that happened. So Snape spent the rest of his life protecting her child, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, who was often said to strongly resemble James. Distrusted for his past as a Death Eater by those on Albus Dumbledore's side, and hated by other Death Eaters for living as Dumbledore's stooge for ten years, Snape continued living on to complete Dumbledore's plan to protect Harry and defeat Voldemort.                
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Between_the_wars_.281981-1995.29">Between the wars <span class="template-c">(1981-1995)</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>You are here to learn the subtle science and exact art of potion-making. As there is little foolish wand-waving here, many of you will hardly believe this is magic. I don't expect you will really understand the beauty of the softly simmering cauldron with its shimmering fumes, the delicate power of liquids that creep through human veins, bewitching the mind, ensnaring the senses... I can teach you how to bottle fame, brew glory, even put a stopper in death — if you aren't as big a bunch of dunderheads as I usually have to teach.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Snape teaching Potions at Hogwarts<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div><figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 162px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Severus-snape1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110316031920" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Severus-snape1"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Severus-snape1.jpg" 	data-image-name="Severus-snape1.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Severus-snape1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/162?cb=20110316031920"  	 width="162"  	 height="233"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Severus-snape1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/162?cb=20110316031920" 	 alt="Severus-snape1"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Severus-snape1.jpg" 	data-image-name="Severus-snape1.jpg" 	 	 width="162"  	 height="233"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Severus-snape1.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Severus Snape, potions master</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
</dd></dl>
<p>When Severus Snape began his teaching career at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> in <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>, taking up a teaching post around the same time as the threat posed by the rampaging curses that had terrorised the castle's residents were contained and the subsequent expulsion of his <a href="/wiki/Jacob_(Hogwarts_student)" title="Jacob (Hogwarts student)">former peer</a> for the rules he had broken in his quest for the Cursed Vaults and the fellow students who had been endangered in the process, he initially applied for the position of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher, but was rejected multiple times.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">[18]</a></sup> Many students were under the impression that this was because Dumbledore feared Snape might return to his old ways if allowed to teach his favourite subject, but in reality it was because Dumbledore was aware by that point that the job had been jinxed by Voldemort. Knowing that no Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher would last longer than a year, Dumbledore instead employed Snape in the position of <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a> and Head of <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin House</a>, following the retirement of veteran Potions Master Professor <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>. Though it seemed rather uncommon for someone as young as Snape to be named Head of any House at Hogwarts, it is possible that Snape was the only Slytherin teacher left at the school, or that he was placed there to keep a watchful eye on the young Slytherins, who were frequently accused of (but not without reason) joining the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>.
</p><p>Following <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s fall, Snape never attempted to find his old master, having switched sides ever since the Dark Lord had targeted Lily and this allowed him to avoid time in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> as Dumbledore staunchly defended him. He fabricated the fact that he believed Voldemort to be dead as an alibi for still loyal Death Eaters, but in truth, he and Dumbledore had discussed Voldemort and knew he would inevitably return, henceforth the most important reason why he applied as a teacher: to ensure from the shadows the safety of Harry Potter, who Lily had died protecting. This would bring him into conflict with fanatical Death Eaters like <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> later in life, but Snape was almost immediately forgiven by the reborn Voldemort, because he could provide him with thirteen years of information on <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 251px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Potions.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161210025049" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Potions"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Potions.jpg" 	data-image-name="Potions.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Potions.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20161210025049"  	 width="251"  	 height="91"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Potions.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20161210025049" 	 alt="Potions"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Potions.jpg" 	data-image-name="Potions.jpg" 	 	 width="251"  	 height="91"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Potions.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape teaching a potions class</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the meantime and with Voldemort vanished, he focused on his teaching duties at Hogwarts. As a professor, Snape was a stickler for discipline, with little patience for foolishness, yet extremely effective in his job and well respected by the other professors. His deep understanding of potion brewing, as shown by his expert concoction of <a href="/wiki/Wolfsbane_Potion" title="Wolfsbane Potion">Wolfsbane Potion</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-18">[19]</a></sup> transformed the knowledge of potions from mere chemistry to an art. This was unfortunate for his classes. He would accept students into his <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.</a> classes only if they had achieved an '<a href="/wiki/Outstanding" title="Outstanding">Outstanding</a>' mark at their <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> examination. He felt that anyone with a lower mark than that would lack the passion and the devotion to the complex and demanding subjects that would follow in the last two years of school. Though strict, Snape had a certain level of bias for Slytherins, giving them undeserved rights over the others, while looking down on the other students somewhat unfairly.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 251px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Severus_Snape_at_Potions_class_%281991%29.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20180608034501" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Severus Snape at Potions class (1991)"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Severus_Snape_at_Potions_class_%281991%29.JPG" 	data-image-name="Severus Snape at Potions class (1991).JPG" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Severus_Snape_at_Potions_class_%281991%29.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180608034501"  	 width="251"  	 height="105"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Severus_Snape_at_Potions_class_%281991%29.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180608034501" 	 alt="Severus Snape at Potions class (1991)"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Severus_Snape_at_Potions_class_%281991%29.JPG" 	data-image-name="Severus Snape at Potions class (1991).JPG" 	 	 width="251"  	 height="105"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Severus_Snape_at_Potions_class_(1991).JPG" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape in his classroom preparing a Potions lesson</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape's role during this entire time was extremely sensitive and required master espionage and image-control skills. As he and Dumbledore anticipated that Voldemort would return eventually, and many of Snape's actions would be reported on by Death Eater spies or gained through torture and <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimency</a>, even if Snape's true mentality and intentions were inaccessible to the Dark Lord, he had to consider every decision and relationship carefully. He treated <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> with maximal coldness and never missed an opportunity to cause him trouble, as any variation from this would have cast suspicion on him in Voldemort's eyes. But in reality, he protected Harry on numerous occasions; he was happy enough to cause the boy, who resembled his father, Snape's hated rival from school days, humiliation and trouble, but never any actual harm or danger as he was still Lily's son. He also had to avoid becoming too aware of Voldemort's plans, so as to avoid being held responsible for allowing Harry and his friends to foil them. But he handled all this brilliantly, and his every action during this period created no mistrust on the part of Voldemort. 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1984-1985_school_year">1984-1985 school year</span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery"><b>Argus Filch</b>: "<i>Is it true that the vaults are filled with gold and powerful prophecies and artefacts from before Hogwarts existed? And that's why that Jacob boy lost his mind trying to find them?</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>Don't worry about what's <b>inside</b> the vaults. Worry about keeping everyone <b>out</b>. Lock the door and keep it guarded.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; Snape and Filch discusses the <a href="/wiki/Cursed_ice" title="Cursed ice">first sign</a> that someone has tampered with the Cursed Vaults<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Hogwarts_Mystery" title="Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div><figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 220px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Screenshot_HM_Y1_sorting_cermony.png/revision/latest?cb=20190508190004" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Screenshot HM Y1 sorting cermony"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Screenshot_HM_Y1_sorting_cermony.png" 	data-image-name="Screenshot HM Y1 sorting cermony.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Screenshot_HM_Y1_sorting_cermony.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190508190004"  	 width="220"  	 height="83"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Screenshot_HM_Y1_sorting_cermony.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190508190004" 	 alt="Screenshot HM Y1 sorting cermony"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Screenshot_HM_Y1_sorting_cermony.png" 	data-image-name="Screenshot HM Y1 sorting cermony.png" 	 	 width="220"  	 height="83"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Screenshot_HM_Y1_sorting_cermony.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape at the Welcoming Feast</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Closing in on the first half a decade of his tenure as an instructor at Hogwarts, Professor Snape was present at the <a href="/wiki/Start-of-Term_Feast" title="Start-of-Term Feast">Start-of-Term Feast</a> of the <a href="/wiki/1984%E2%80%931985_school_year" title="1984–1985 school year">1984–1985 school year</a>, during which he was introduced to the new <a href="/wiki/First_Year" title="First Year" class="mw-redirect">First Years</a> as the <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Slytherin_House" title="Head of Slytherin House">Head of Slytherin House</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">Sorting ceremony</a>. He witnessed the sorting of, among others, the <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob's sibling">younger sibling</a> of Jacob, who was sorted into the same house as Jacob and of whom he became immediately suspicious.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[20]</a></sup> During the very first day of teaching the first years, he instructed the newcomers in the correct way in which to brew a <a href="/wiki/Cure_for_Boils" title="Cure for Boils">Cure for Boils</a>, during which he made no attempt at hiding his dislike for Jacob's cognate, and openly favoured <a href="/wiki/Merula_Snyde" title="Merula Snyde">Merula Snyde</a>, a student in his own house and whose parents had been among his own comrades during his time as a Death Eater, presumably both due to his bias towards his own house, as well as part of maintaining his cover as a future double agent. Throughout the year, he proceeded to teach this class, among other things, the <a href="/wiki/Wiggenweld_Potion" title="Wiggenweld Potion">Wiggenweld Potion</a><sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[21]</a></sup>, the <a href="/wiki/Herbicide_Potion" title="Herbicide Potion">Herbicide Potion</a><sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">[22]</a></sup> and how to properly concoct a <a href="/wiki/Sleeping_Draught" title="Sleeping Draught">Sleeping Draught</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">[23]</a></sup> Throughout the term, however, Professor Snape found himself reluctantly acknowledging the said student's talent.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/Harry-Potter-Hogwarts-Mystery-Mobile-Game-2018-Portkey-Games-Warner-Bros-iOS-Android-Free-to-Play-Severus-Snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180803110049" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/Harry-Potter-Hogwarts-Mystery-Mobile-Game-2018-Portkey-Games-Warner-Bros-iOS-Android-Free-to-Play-Severus-Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180803110049" 	 alt="Harry-Potter-Hogwarts-Mystery-Mobile-Game-2018-Portkey-Games-Warner-Bros-iOS-Android-Free-to-Play-Severus-Snape"  	class="thumbimage " 	data-image-name="Harry-Potter-Hogwarts-Mystery-Mobile-Game-2018-Portkey-Games-Warner-Bros-iOS-Android-Free-to-Play-Severus-Snape.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-Potter-Hogwarts-Mystery-Mobile-Game-2018-Portkey-Games-Warner-Bros-iOS-Android-Free-to-Play-Severus-Snape.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape in the 1980s</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sometime later, Snape and the school's <a href="/wiki/Charms_Master" title="Charms Master">Charms Master</a> <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a> were made aware of how there were to be an unsanctioned duel between <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob's sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> and Merula Snyde in the <a href="/wiki/Clock_Tower_Courtyard" title="Clock Tower Courtyard">Clocktower Courtyard</a>, arriving just in time to see the latter successfully deprive their opponent of her wand. Although Professor <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a> wanted to know who it was that cast the first spell, keeping in mind that Jacob's sibling had been instructed to only ever use the <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charm</a> defensively, Snape was largely dismissive of who started the fight. After subtly criticising his colleague, whom he correctly deduced were the one who had instructed said student in how to cast the <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charm</a> in the first place, he ordered both students to get cleaned up and meet up at the <a href="/wiki/West_Tower" title="West Tower">West Tower</a> in order to receive punishment for their transgression. Upon reporting the incident to <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, Snape asked for Jacob's sibling to be expelled, whom he regarded as a troublemaker just like their brother before them, a request the Headmaster rejected, and which he would soon thereafter lament about in the presence of both Jacob's sibling and Snyde. Although he docked twenty points from the former's house, he was interrupted by the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Caretaker" title="Hogwarts Caretaker">Caretaker</a> of the day, <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a>, before he could do anything else. Upon being informed about an incident that had occurred that demanded his immediate attention that was related to the Cursed Vaults, Snape ordered both students to return to their <a href="/wiki/Common_Room" title="Common Room" class="mw-redirect">Common Rooms</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">[24]</a></sup>
</p><p>Accompanying the Caretaker to a corridor on the fifth floor, Mr Filch explained that he and his pet cat, <a href="/wiki/Mrs_Norris" title="Mrs Norris">Mrs Norris</a>, had discovered how <a href="/wiki/Cursed_ice" title="Cursed ice">Cursed ice</a> had appeared in one of the rooms there. Immediately recognising this as one of the curses unleashed when someone had tampered with the Cursed Vaults, Snape immediately ordered Filch to lock the door and stand guard to prevent students from getting inside, before he left to inform the Headmaster. In the aftermath of this discovery, the faculty successfully managed to keep it from spreading any further and securely sealed up the room afterwards, although he was unaware the two students he had just left had followed them and overheard portions of his conversation with Filch and resolved to break into the room in order to look for clues regarding the whereabouts of the vaults.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">[25]</a></sup> Throughout the rest of the year, he presumably continued to keep a sharp eye on the students, especially Jacob's sibling, and do everything he could to keep the discovery from the student body, in which he was ultimately unsuccessful.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">[26]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1985-1986_school_year">1985-1986 school year</span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">"<i>I mentioned <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> in Potions, and Snape threw a jar of pickled animal parts at me.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Unidentified first year<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Hogwarts_Mystery" title="Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>At some point early on in the year, Snape became livid when a <a href="/wiki/First_year" title="First year">first-year</a> mentioned <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> in class, and hurled a jar of pickled animal parts at him.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">[27]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1991-1992_school_year">1991-1992 school year</span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone"><b>Snape</b>: "<i>You don't want me as your enemy, Quirrell.</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Quirinus Quirrell</b>: "<i>I-I don't know what you —</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>You know perfectly well what I mean.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; A warning after Quirrell attempted to seize the Philosopher's Stone<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div><figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 266px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f5/Hooch_welcoming_feast.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160723002756" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Hooch welcoming feast"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Hooch_welcoming_feast.jpg" 	data-image-name="Hooch welcoming feast.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f5/Hooch_welcoming_feast.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/266?cb=20160723002756"  	 width="266"  	 height="115"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f5/Hooch_welcoming_feast.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/266?cb=20160723002756" 	 alt="Hooch welcoming feast"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Hooch_welcoming_feast.jpg" 	data-image-name="Hooch welcoming feast.jpg" 	 	 width="266"  	 height="115"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hooch_welcoming_feast.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape sitting with Quirinus Quirrell and Rolanda Hooch at the start of the 1991 school year</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicolas Flamel</a>, a famous alchemist and friend of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, had the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher's Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a> that was keeping him alive moved from his safe in <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts</a> to Hogwarts for safekeeping. Snape contributed to the defences set up around the magical artefact by adding a Potions Riddle as one of the obstacles, and the only obstacle that used logic as a key factor instead of magic. At the same time, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> became a student in Snape's classes, and the two of them detested each other almost immediately. Harry's resemblance to <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">his father</a> and his acquired 'celebrity' status brought the worst out of Snape from their very first <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> lesson. Although Snape had pledged an oath to Dumbledore that he would protect Harry, such an oath did not stand in the way of Snape's bias to Slytherin House, nor did it mean Harry was to get any special treatment in academics.
</p><p>Throughout the year as part of his promise to Dumbledore, Snape did everything he could to prevent <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Professor Quirinus Quirrell</a> from helping <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> obtain the Philosopher's Stone, having seen him as what he was and at least knew he was helping Voldemort, if not also being aware of Voldemort possessing Quirell. By <a href="/wiki/31_October" title="31 October">31 October</a>, the turbaned Professor, sure enough, made his first move by letting a <a href="/wiki/Mountain_troll" title="Mountain troll">Mountain Troll</a> into <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Castle" title="Hogwarts Castle">Hogwarts Castle</a> as a diversion. Snape took this chance to stop him from sneaking into the <a href="/wiki/Third-floor_corridor" title="Third-floor corridor">restricted third-floor corridor</a> where the Stone was being hidden in the midst of the chaotic event, only to get bitten in the leg by the corridor's <a href="/wiki/Three-headed_dog" title="Three-headed dog">three-headed guard dog</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fluffy" title="Fluffy">Fluffy</a>.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 240px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150811182354" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20150811182354"  	 width="240"  	 height="119"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20150811182354" 	 alt="Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg" 	 	 width="240"  	 height="119"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape saving Harry's life during a Quidditch game</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Quirrell made his first attempt on Harry's life by jinxing <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_Nimbus_2000" title="Harry Potter's Nimbus 2000">his new broomstick</a> during the boy's first <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> game, Snape intervened again by performing a <a href="/wiki/Counter-curse" title="Counter-curse">counter-curse</a> to prevent Harry from being hurled off. Unfortunately, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> observed the crowd through binoculars to figure out who was performing the jinx and caught Snape discreetly uttering the counter-curse incantation, but erroneously thought he was performing the actual curse. So she ran to his stand and set fire to his robes in order to distract him and make him stop, and luckily for Snape, she accidentally knocked Quirrell over during her hurry back to the Gryffindor stands, causing him to break the eye contact necessary for performing his spell correctly. For the next match, Snape insisted on refereeing to make sure it did not happen again. This did not come across well to the other teachers, who believed that he was just trying to injure the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a>'s chances of winning.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 264px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Snape_and_quirrell.png/revision/latest?cb=20131016224556" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Snape and quirrell"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Snape_and_quirrell.png" 	data-image-name="Snape and quirrell.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Snape_and_quirrell.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/264?cb=20131016224556"  	 width="264"  	 height="117"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Snape_and_quirrell.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/264?cb=20131016224556" 	 alt="Snape and quirrell"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Snape_and_quirrell.png" 	data-image-name="Snape and quirrell.png" 	 	 width="264"  	 height="117"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape_and_quirrell.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape confronting Quirrell during the night</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>Snape intensely confronted Quirrell in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> on the night after the match, demanding to know why he was after the Philosopher's Stone. Unbeknownst to them both, Harry was watching the entire argument from the treetops, having followed his Potions teacher into the forest on his broomstick after passing him at the school <a href="/wiki/Quidditch_Changing_Rooms" title="Quidditch Changing Rooms">Quidditch shed</a>. But because the boy suspected Snape of plotting to steal the stone and of attempting to kill him, it seemed to him that the Potions professor was trying to intimidate Quirrell into handing over information regarding the artefact. So he, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> and Hermione unjustly tried to be supportive and encouraging to Quirrell whenever possible by telling people off for laughing at his stutter, smiling at him encouragingly whenever they passed him or arguing with Snape.
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1992-1993_school_year">1992-1993 school year</span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Maybe he's left, because he missed out on the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> job again!</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>Or he might have been sacked! I mean, everyone hates him —</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>Or maybe he's waiting to hear why you two didn't arrive on the school train.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; Confronting Harry and Ron after they arrive via a flying car<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div><figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 244px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2e/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-3935.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170703224045" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-3935"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-3935.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-3935.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2e/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-3935.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/244?cb=20170703224045"  	 width="244"  	 height="98"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2e/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-3935.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/244?cb=20170703224045" 	 alt="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-3935"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-3935.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-3935.jpg" 	 	 width="244"  	 height="98"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-3935.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry Potter and Ron Weasley in Snape's office after being seen by Muggles driving a flying Ford Anglia</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the beginning of the school year in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>, Snape learned from the <i><a href="/wiki/Evening_Prophet" title="Evening Prophet">Evening Prophet</a></i> that Muggles spotted Harry and Ron travelling to Hogwarts in a <a href="/wiki/Flying_Ford_Anglia" title="Flying Ford Anglia">flying Ford Anglia</a>, instead of on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>. Knowing the severity of their deeds could very well cause them to be expelled, which would put Harry in great danger as he would lose Dumbledore's protection, Snape took matters into his hand and confronted them when they had landed, where he severely berated them for their breach of one of the most sacred laws of their world and pretended to call upon Professors Dumbledore and <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> to make them solve this situation. It was as Snape wanted: Dumbledore ensured they would not be expelled and Minerva punished them instead by giving them a warning and separate detentions.
