</p><p>Regardless of his desire to uphold Lily's memory, Snape considered the punishment too lenient and retaliated by allowing the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin_Quidditch_team" title="Slytherin Quidditch team">Slytherin Quidditch team</a> to unfairly usurp the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Quidditch_pitch" title="Hogwarts Quidditch pitch">Hogwarts Quidditch pitch</a> during the Gryffindor team's practice time. This was in order for them to train <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> as their new <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a>. Later on in the year, Harry, Ron, and Hermione successfully managed to smuggle <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> ingredients from Snape's personal cabinets. They did this by creating a spectacle of a diversion in his classroom, which involved a firecracker and the <a href="/wiki/Swelling_Solution" title="Swelling Solution">Swelling Potion</a> that was being made in class. He was utterly furious at the mess and the way he looked it Harry made it clear he knew it was Harry who had caused it considering the way he looked at Harry, with Harry referring to having felt Snape read his mind, strongly indicating Snape used <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimency</a> on him. However, he was forced to let Harry go again as Dumbledore had made it clear to him that no other punishment but being expelled would be dealt out to Harry if he broke another rule and Snape could not let his anger overpower his desire to see Lily's son be protected.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170718022052" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Harry-potter2-movie-duel"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170718022052"  	 width="250"  	 height="100"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170718022052" 	 alt="Harry-potter2-movie-duel"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg" 	 	 width="250"  	 height="100"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape prepares to duel Lockhart during the first and last Duelling Club meeting</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During this year, Professor Snape also worked with the new <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor, <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>, in running the <a href="/wiki/Duelling_Club" title="Duelling Club">Duelling Club</a>. In this period, he quickly visibly showed a large amount of irritation and anger at Professor Lockhart who would remain, evermore, the teacher of the subject he most cherished. Snape took a certain amount of enjoyment in blasting him against a wall and looking ready to murder him on the spot to the point that even Lockhart was intimidated enough to stop annoying Snape. He ensured that Harry would be engaged with Draco instead, but interfered when Harry and Draco practically checkmated each other, with Harry using the <a href="/wiki/Tickling_Charm" title="Tickling Charm">Tickling Charm</a> on Malfoy and was subsequently hit by the <a href="/wiki/Dancing_Feet_Spell" title="Dancing Feet Spell">Dancing Feet Spell</a>. Although he gave Malfoy the instruction needed to conjure a snake and relished the fact that Harry was alone to face the large angry snake, once Harry showed his <a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">Parseltongue</a> ability, Snape quickly interfered to avoid too much of a problem on Harry's part by vanishing the snake and allowing him to be escorted out of the Great Hall by his friends but looked at him suspiciously before he left.
</p><p>Lockhart would only further irritate Professor Snape during <a href="/wiki/Valentine%27s_Day" title="Valentine's Day">Valentine's Day</a>, where he held a party to celebrate it as Snape looked on particularly dreadfully to the point he looked as if he had been forced to take multiple <a href="/wiki/Skele-Gro" title="Skele-Gro">Skele-Gro</a> and Snape did not hesitate to look utterly infuriated when Lockhart cheerfully asked the students to make Snape brew for them <a href="/wiki/Love_Potion" title="Love Potion">Love Potions</a> to the point he clearly shot a warning look to them that he would force-feed anyone who dared to ask him to poison. Snape was very likely among the professors who were highly irritated by the Cupids Lockhart unleashed upon Hogwarts as they keep getting in the way of lessons. This hatred for Lockhart finally reached its apex when Professor Lockhart walked in upon their discovery of Ginny being taken to the Chamber of Secrets, as even Snape was genuinely concerned for her regardless of how he treated Gryffindor, and furiously led the teachers into forcing him out of the way so that students could be escorted to safety, outright not giving Lockhart even a second to rebuke Snape's claim of having heard Lockhart proclaim that he had found the monster.
</p><p>By describing the <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> in Potions class (which Hermione remembered), and demonstrating the Disarming Charm to the Duelling Club, Snape taught Harry two skills that ultimately proved critical to his success.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1993-1994_school_year">1993-1994 school year</span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>Well, well, well, I never thought I'd meet a third-year class who wouldn't even recognise a <a href="/wiki/Lycanthropy" title="Lycanthropy">werewolf</a> when they saw one. I shall make a point of informing Professor Dumbledore how very behind you all are.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Snape substituting as the DADA professor<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>During this school year, Snape demonstrated his expertise with potions by brewing the complex <a href="/wiki/Wolfsbane_Potion" title="Wolfsbane Potion">Wolfsbane Potion</a> for the new <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor, <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>. Throughout this year, Snape suspected that Lupin may be helping <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, an escapee from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>, enter Hogwarts castle. This suspicion stemmed from Lupin's friendship with Sirius and Harry's father <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a> when they were all at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> as students. It is revealed that Sirius once played a joke on Snape, telling him that he could find out where Lupin was going every month if he climbed into the <a href="/wiki/Whomping_Willow" title="Whomping Willow">Whomping Willow</a>. James realised the danger and saved Snape's life by pulling him back.
</dd></dl>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 245px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/63/Harry-potter4-movie-screencaps.com-11140.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150811180558" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Harry-potter4-movie-screencaps.com-11140"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Harry-potter4-movie-screencaps.com-11140.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry-potter4-movie-screencaps.com-11140.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/63/Harry-potter4-movie-screencaps.com-11140.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20150811180558"  	 width="245"  	 height="114"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/63/Harry-potter4-movie-screencaps.com-11140.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20150811180558" 	 alt="Harry-potter4-movie-screencaps.com-11140"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Harry-potter4-movie-screencaps.com-11140.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry-potter4-movie-screencaps.com-11140.jpg" 	 	 width="245"  	 height="114"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter4-movie-screencaps.com-11140.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape confronts Sirius and Lupin in the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Near the end of the school year, Snape ambushed Black as he entered the school again and attempted to apprehend him, believing him to have been the one who had betrayed Lily to Voldemort. Snape appeared from under the <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Invisibility cloak</a> that Harry had left near the Whomping Willow, tied Remus up, and while engaged in a vociferous argument with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> and Hermione, he attempted to arrange to send Sirius and Remus to Azkaban Prison. However, before he could give Sirius and Remus to the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a>, Harry, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> simultaneously used Expelliarmus on Snape. Snape also said that Harry, Ron, and Hermione faced suspension for being out-of-bounds. Since Harry aided Black's escape, Snape was beside himself with indignation. On the last day of school, he revealed to his students that Lupin was a werewolf, forcing Lupin to resign his post.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1994-1995_school_year">1994-1995 school year</span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"'<i>Course Dumbledore trusts you. He's a trusting man, isn't he? Believes in second chances. But me — I say there are spots that don't come off, Snape. <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark#On_the_arm" title="Dark Mark">Spots that never come off</a>, d'you know what I mean?</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a> <span class="template-c">(as Alastor Moody)</span> referring to Snape's Dark Mark<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div><figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 251px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/11_1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160114192835" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="11 1"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="11_1.jpg" 	data-image-name="11 1.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/11_1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20160114192835"  	 width="251"  	 height="107"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/11_1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20160114192835" 	 alt="11 1"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="11_1.jpg" 	data-image-name="11 1.jpg" 	 	 width="251"  	 height="107"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:11_1.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape and others' reactions after Harry Potter is selected as the fourth Triwizard champion</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
</dd></dl>
<p>Snape was apoplectic when Harry's name was unexpectedly chosen from the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a>. Despite the fishy circumstances surrounding the incident and the immense dangers that Harry was facing, Snape refused to believe that he did not deliberately enter himself in for the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>. Indeed, he continued to treat Harry as maliciously as ever, thinking that he had broken into his office to steal ingredients that would aid him in the underwater phase of the tournament.
</p><p>Harry later discovered that Snape was once a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> but had been vouched for by Dumbledore. Dumbledore told the <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a> that although Snape had indeed worked for Voldemort, he changed sides and turned spy against him. Dumbledore reassured Harry that Snape's loyalties were genuine, though he refused to tell Harry why.
</p><p>Harry was not the only one who had expressed scepticism over Snape's reform. <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Professor Moody</a> had Snape's office searched at the beginning of the year, claiming that it was an "Auror's privilege" and that Dumbledore mentioned being watchful of him. Snape was resentful of Moody's accusations but could not do anything about it. (In truth, Moody was actually an impostor who had been raiding Snape's cabinet for ingredients to make <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a>.)
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 251px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170718015710" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20170718015710"  	 width="251"  	 height="106"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20170718015710" 	 alt="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg" 	 	 width="251"  	 height="106"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Karkaroff</a> showing Snape his Dark Mark</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Despite Snape's unawareness of the real reason why Harry was in the tournament, it had not escaped his notice that Lord Voldemort's mark was becoming increasingly more pronounced throughout the year. Karkaroff, who dreaded retribution from Voldemort, panicked and confided his fears in Snape. Karkaroff attempted to talk to him numerous times throughout the year, but Snape had no sympathy for him and offered no help. Karkaroff consequently fled when the Dark Lord returned, but Snape, who remained in the Dark Lord's good favour with the information he could provide on Dumbledore, had nothing to fear from him in the term of retribution. In fact, he appeared to have been waiting for Voldemort's return more than ever in this year, as he and Dumbledore were conversing about it.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest?cb=20180423221722" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="B4C36M1 Snape Dark Mark reveal"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" 	data-image-name="B4C36M1 Snape Dark Mark reveal.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722"  	 width="250"  	 height="102"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" 	 alt="B4C36M1 Snape Dark Mark reveal"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" 	data-image-name="B4C36M1 Snape Dark Mark reveal.png" 	 	 width="250"  	 height="102"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape uses his Dark Mark as proof that <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> has returned</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament#The_Third_Task" title="Triwizard Tournament">Third Task</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Return_of_Lord_Voldemort" title="Return of Lord Voldemort">Rebirth of Lord Voldemort</a>, Barty Crouch Jnr took Harry to Moody's office. Crouch Jnr started to question Harry about what had happened but was shortly rescued by Professors Dumbledore, McGonagall, and Snape. Soon the effects of Crouch Jnr's Polyjuice Potion wore off; in the excitement, he had neglected to take it at the proper time to maintain his cover. Under the effects of <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a> provided by Professor Snape, Crouch described Lord Voldemort's plan to resurrect himself and Crouch Jnr's own involvement in getting Harry to the graveyard. Dumbledore and Snape attempted to convince a disbelieving <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> that Voldemort had returned. Snape was finally told the truth about Sirius's innocence and was forced by Dumbledore to shake hands. He was subsequently sent on a secret mission by Dumbledore to rejoin the Death Eaters and spy on the Dark Lord as a re-doubled agent.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_Wizarding_War_.281995-1998.29">Second Wizarding War <span class="template-c">(1995-1998)</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1995-1996_school_year">1995-1996 school year</span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)"><b>Dolores Umbridge</b>: "<i>Ah, yes. The time has come for answers, whether he wants to give them or not. Have you bought the Veritaserum?</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>I'm afraid you have used up all my stores interrogating students... Unless you wish to poison Potter — and I assure you, I would have the greatest sympathy if you did — I cannot help you.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; Snape witholding Veritaserum from Umbridge<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div>During the 1995-1996 school year, with Voldemort having returned to his body, Snape carried on with his work as a re-doubled agent for Dumbledore. During the summer, he was seen at <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> giving reports to the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. Snape frequently taunted Sirius about the latter not being able to take an active role in the Order's missions due to his fugitive status.
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161121214826" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg" 	data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161121214826"  	 width="250"  	 height="110"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161121214826" 	 alt="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg" 	data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg" 	 	 width="250"  	 height="110"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry's first Occlumency lesson with Snape</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Back at school, Snape's allegiance to the Order had no effect on his dislike for <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>. When Harry began having visions about Lord Voldemort, Dumbledore asked Snape to teach Harry <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> in order to shut down the telepathic connection.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-27">[28]</a></sup> However, mutual hostility made it difficult for them to work productively during the sessions. Indeed, Snape had to be very careful in the ways that he helped Harry, should Voldemort read Harry's mind and discover his servant working against him. At one point, Harry peeked into the <a href="/wiki/Pensieve" title="Pensieve">Pensieve</a> when Snape was out of his office and witnessed a private memory of Snape being viciously bullied and harassed by <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">Harry's father</a>. Upon returning, Snape grabbed him roughly by the arm and threw him out of the office and forbade him from ever coming back again. For all the rest of that semester, he treated Harry with redoubled contempt and fury and ignored him in class whenever possible. 
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180203175328" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg" 	data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180203175328"  	 width="250"  	 height="116"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180203175328" 	 alt="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg" 	data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg" 	 	 width="250"  	 height="116"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><span><i>"</i></span><i>He's got <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Padfoot</a> at the place where it's hidden.<span>"</span></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Towards the end of the school year, <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> captured Harry and questioned him on the whereabouts of Dumbledore. She sent for Snape to provide <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a> to force Harry to reveal any information he may be hiding. Snape claimed that his supplies of Veritaserum were exhausted earlier, when she had attempted to use the drug surreptitiously to force information from Harry (however, it is highly likely that he lied). As a result, Snape withheld further assistance.
</p><p>It is later revealed that Snape had actually given Umbridge a fake potion during her prior attempts. Upon hearing Harry's cryptic warning about Sirius's capture, he swiftly carried the message back to the other Order members, and helped come up with a plan for them to come to the rescue in the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Mysteries" title="Department of Mysteries">Department of Mysteries</a> while he searched the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> for Harry. But since Umbridge was near, he pretended to ignore it. However, despite the fact that Snape came to his aid multiple times throughout the year, Harry hated him as much as ever, due to believing that Snape's goading spurred Sirius into joining the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">battle</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1996-1997_school_year">1996-1997 school year</span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>Severus... please....</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Dumbledore pleading for Snape to end his life<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div><figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 245px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/Unbreakable_vow.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140918121231" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Unbreakable vow"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Unbreakable_vow.gif" 	data-image-name="Unbreakable vow.gif" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/Unbreakable_vow.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140918121231"  	 width="245"  	 height="108"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/Unbreakable_vow.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140918121231" 	 alt="Unbreakable vow"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Unbreakable_vow.gif" 	data-image-name="Unbreakable vow.gif" 	 	 width="245"  	 height="108"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Unbreakable_vow.gif" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape and <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa Malfoy</a> making an Unbreakable Vow, with Bellatrix Lestrange as the bonding agent</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>In July 1996 Dumbledore had been afflicted by a <a href="/wiki/Curse_on_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_ring" title="Curse on Marvolo Gaunt's ring">powerful curse</a> cast on <a href="/wiki/Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_ring" title="Marvolo Gaunt's ring" class="mw-redirect">Marvolo Gaunt's ring</a>, one of Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, prior to the start of Harry's sixth year at Hogwarts. Although Snape's knowledge of the Dark Arts enabled him to slow the spread of the curse, the curse would have ultimately killed Dumbledore within a year. Dumbledore, aware that Voldemort had ordered Draco to kill him, asked Snape to kill him instead as a way of sparing the boy's soul and of preventing his own otherwise slow, painful death. Although Snape was reluctant, even asking about the impact of such an action on his own soul, Dumbledore implied that this kind of coup de grâce would not damage a human's <a href="/wiki/Soul" title="Soul">soul</a> in the same way murder would. Furthermore, once Snape had done the deed, he would gain Voldemort's complete trust and learn more of his plans. Snape agreed to do as the Headmaster requested.
</dd></dl>
<p>Shortly after that, Snape was visited by <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> and <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa Malfoy</a> at his home in <a href="/wiki/Spinner%27s_End" title="Spinner's End">Spinner's End</a>. Narcissa's son <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco</a> had been given a difficult task by Voldemort, and Narcissa swore Snape to an <a href="/wiki/Unbreakable_Vow" title="Unbreakable Vow">Unbreakable Vow</a>, on pain of death should he break it, that he would protect Draco, help him complete Voldemort's task, and finish the task himself if Draco failed. When questioned by Bellatrix about his loyalties, Snape claimed to have been working for Voldemort (rather than for Dumbledore) ever since Voldemort's return, and explained his actions in the previous years in that light. In addition, he pointed out that Dumbledore's protection had kept him out of <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> and free to operate on Voldemort's behalf.
</p><p>At the start-of-term feast at Hogwarts, Dumbledore announced he had finally appointed Snape as Professor of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>, much to Harry's shock and displeasure. Snape was no less severe in teaching Defence than he had been with Potions, although he did allow students who achieved below "Outstanding" at <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> level to enter his <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.</a> classes. Having finally acquired the position he desired for so long, Snape taught the lessons with a tone of passion for the Dark Arts he sought to undo, something he did not do for Potions. He also became less biased, as he allowed Hermione to answer his question (as opposed to three years ago, he insulted her for being "an insufferable know-it-all"), and sentenced Crabbe and Goyle to detention for dissatisfying progress in their repeated <a href="/wiki/Fifth_year" title="Fifth year">fifth year</a>.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/SeverusSnape_WB_F6_SnapeAndDracoInHallway_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190209142010" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="SeverusSnape WB F6 SnapeAndDracoInHallway Still 080615 Land"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="SeverusSnape_WB_F6_SnapeAndDracoInHallway_Still_080615_Land.jpg" 	data-image-name="SeverusSnape WB F6 SnapeAndDracoInHallway Still 080615 Land.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/SeverusSnape_WB_F6_SnapeAndDracoInHallway_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190209142010"  	 width="250"  	 height="141"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/SeverusSnape_WB_F6_SnapeAndDracoInHallway_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190209142010" 	 alt="SeverusSnape WB F6 SnapeAndDracoInHallway Still 080615 Land"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="SeverusSnape_WB_F6_SnapeAndDracoInHallway_Still_080615_Land.jpg" 	data-image-name="SeverusSnape WB F6 SnapeAndDracoInHallway Still 080615 Land.jpg" 	 	 width="250"  	 height="141"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:SeverusSnape_WB_F6_SnapeAndDracoInHallway_Still_080615_Land.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape offering Draco Malfoy assistance with his mission</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, a retired Hogwarts teacher, replaced Snape as Potions Master. Slughorn loaned Harry an <a href="/wiki/Half-Blood_Prince%27s_copy_of_Advanced_Potion-Making" title="Half-Blood Prince's copy of Advanced Potion-Making" class="mw-redirect">old Potions textbook</a>, in which Harry found marginalia including helpful tips on how to make potions better and a variety of hexes and jinxes seemingly invented by an unknown student. The book was inscribed "<i>This Book is the Property of the Half-Blood Prince</i>". With the help of the notes, Harry quickly became the best potion-maker in the class and Slughorn's favourite student. Snape, however, was suspicious when he heard about Harry's newfound success, maintaining that he <i>"never had the impression that [he] had been able to teach Potter anything at all</i>".
</p><p>In the spring, Snape met with Dumbledore on the outskirts of the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> and wanted to know more about the private lessons between Albus and Harry. Not knowing that they were overheard by Hagrid, Snape burst into resentment that Dumbledore trusts Harry more than him. Dumbledore only ordered Severus to look after Draco even more, after <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> has been poisoned. Albus also invited him for an evening visit in <a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_office" title="Headmaster's office" class="mw-redirect">his office</a>. When Snape arrived and learned that Harry had to die, he showed outrage and ultimately showed that he still after all these years loved <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily</a> by revealing his <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> to be a doe, the same as Lily's.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 220px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cb/Vulnera_Sanentur.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20100811181504" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Vulnera Sanentur"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Vulnera_Sanentur.JPG" 	data-image-name="Vulnera Sanentur.JPG" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cb/Vulnera_Sanentur.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20100811181504"  	 width="220"  	 height="98"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cb/Vulnera_Sanentur.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20100811181504" 	 alt="Vulnera Sanentur"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Vulnera_Sanentur.JPG" 	data-image-name="Vulnera Sanentur.JPG" 	 	 width="220"  	 height="98"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vulnera_Sanentur.JPG" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape healing Draco's wounds</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later, in a fight with Draco, Harry cast one of the Prince's spells marked "For Enemies" (<i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i>) and was horrified when it caused devastating wounds to Draco's face and chest. Snape rushed to the scene and <a href="/wiki/Vulnera_Sanentur" title="Vulnera Sanentur">healed Draco's wounds</a>, and then interrogated Harry about the source of the spell. When Harry refused to tell him anything, Snape demanded that he bring him all of his books. Harry hid the Prince's book and gave Ron Weasley's copy of the book to Snape instead. Snape punished Harry by giving him a detention every Saturday for the rest of the year, including during the final <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> match of the season. Fearing of exposing himself as the inventor of the curse that injured Draco, Snape did not outright expose Harry's cheating in Potions to Slughorn or the rest of the staff, thus resulting in a punishment much more lenient than usual, which Professor McGonagall saw as something very lucky for Harry.
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a></i></div>
</dd></dl>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 245px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Dumbledore_dies.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140813154818" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Dumbledore dies"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Dumbledore_dies.gif" 	data-image-name="Dumbledore dies.gif" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Dumbledore_dies.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140813154818"  	 width="245"  	 height="150"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Dumbledore_dies.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140813154818" 	 alt="Dumbledore dies"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Dumbledore_dies.gif" 	data-image-name="Dumbledore dies.gif" 	 	 width="245"  	 height="150"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_dies.gif" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape proves his loyalty to Dumbledore - by ending the headmaster's life as requested</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Before leaving with Dumbledore to find a <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>, Harry discovered from <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Professor Sybill Trelawney</a> that it had been Severus who overheard the <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney's first prophecy">Prophecy</a> and told it to Voldemort, thus causing Voldemort to hunt Harry and his parents. Despite this and Harry's angry questions, Dumbledore maintained that he trusted Snape. After returning to Hogwarts with the Slytherin Locket, Harry and Dumbledore flew to the school's <a href="/wiki/Astronomy_Tower" title="Astronomy Tower">Astronomy Tower</a>. Gravely weakened by Voldemort's potion, and the school being under attack by Death Eaters, Dumbledore asked Harry to fetch Snape for him. Before Harry could leave, Draco arrived and <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">disarmed</a> Dumbledore, intending to carry out Voldemort's ordered assassination. Draco was unable to bring himself to commit the murder, however, and Snape killed the headmaster himself.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Snape_vs_Harry.gif/revision/latest?cb=20090609234006" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Snape vs Harry"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Snape_vs_Harry.gif" 	data-image-name="Snape vs Harry.gif" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Snape_vs_Harry.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090609234006"  	 width="250"  	 height="106"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Snape_vs_Harry.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090609234006" 	 alt="Snape vs Harry"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Snape_vs_Harry.gif" 	data-image-name="Snape vs Harry.gif" 	 	 width="250"  	 height="106"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape_vs_Harry.gif" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">"<i>You dare use my own spells against me, Potter? It was I who invented them — I, the Half-Blood Prince!</i>"</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>An enraged Harry (who had been <a href="/wiki/Full_Body-Bind_Curse" title="Full Body-Bind Curse">immobilised</a> by Dumbledore for his own protection and had witnessed the killing while under his <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Invisibility cloak</a>) chased Snape, Draco, and the Death Eaters as they fled the castle. The two of them engaged in a fierce duel, which became increasingly one-sided. Snape easily blocked Harry's attempts to attack him and jeeringly pointed out Harry's mistakes, but refused to strike back. However, he became enraged when Harry called him a coward and began using his own spells against him, resulting in him blasting Harry back against the ground.
</p><p>During the confrontation, Snape also revealed himself to be the "Half-Blood Prince" (being the son of <a href="/wiki/Tobias_Snape" title="Tobias Snape">Tobias Snape</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Eileen_Prince" title="Eileen Prince">Eileen Prince</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a>). Harry was unable to stop Snape before the latter passed through the school gates and <a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Disapparated</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="On_the_run">On the run</span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>I don't think he wanted to associate himself with that book. I don't think Dumbledore would have liked it very much if he'd known. And even if Snape pretended it hadn't been his, Slughorn would have recognised his writing at once.</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>I should have showed the book to Dumbledore. All that time he was showing me how Voldemort was evil even when he was at school, and I had proof Snape was, too —</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; Upon finding out Snape was the owner of the <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_copy_of_Advanced_Potion-Making" title="Severus Snape's copy of Advanced Potion-Making">textbook</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div><figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811152234" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Meeting at Malfoy Manor"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor.jpg" 	data-image-name="Meeting at Malfoy Manor.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/247?cb=20180811152234"  	 width="247"  	 height="103"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/247?cb=20180811152234" 	 alt="Meeting at Malfoy Manor"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor.jpg" 	data-image-name="Meeting at Malfoy Manor.jpg" 	 	 width="247"  	 height="103"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Severus at the Death Eater <a href="/wiki/Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Meeting at Malfoy Manor">Meeting at Malfoy Manor</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After killing Albus Dumbledore and fleeing the school, Snape once more rejoined the ranks of the Death Eaters. In the summer of 1997, Snape informed Lord Voldemort that Harry was to depart from his <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">relatives</a>' <a href="/wiki/4_Privet_Drive" title="4 Privet Drive">house</a> four days before his birthday. On Dumbledore's orders, Snape told the Death Eaters the correct date so as to continue Voldemort's trust in him.
</p><p>Snape then fed <a href="/wiki/Mundungus_Fletcher" title="Mundungus Fletcher">Mundungus Fletcher</a> the idea of using seven decoys of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> during his movement to a place of safety so that when the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> arrived, they would not know who the real one was. In order to be consistent in his own role as a Death Eater, Snape <a href="/wiki/Confundus_Charm" title="Confundus Charm">confunded</a> Fletcher so that he would not remember who told him.
</p><p>Because of Severus' information, when the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> moved Harry from Privet Drive they were ambushed by Death Eaters, and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a> ensued. During the battle, Snape accidentally sliced <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a>'s ear off with his wand while aiming at another Death Eater.
</p><p>Shortly after the battle, Severus visited <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> where, in <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black%27s_bedroom" title="Sirius Black's bedroom">Sirius Black' bedroom</a>, he found <a href="/wiki/Lily_Potter%27s_letter" title="Lily Potter's letter" class="mw-redirect">Lily Potter's letter</a>. Snape had cut off the letter and took the page, which contained Lily's signature and love. He also cut off the picture of <a href="/wiki/Potter_family" title="Potter family">Potter family</a> and took the page, which contained Lily, for himself.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="As_Headmaster">As Headmaster</span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Severus Snape, long-standing Potions master at Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and wizardry, was today appointed Headmaster in the most important of several staffing changes at the ancient school. Following the resignation of the previous Muggle Studies teacher, Alecto Carrow will take over the post while her brother, Amycus, fills the position of Defence Against the Dark Arts professor. 'I welcome the opportunity to uphold our finest Wizarding traditions and values' —</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;<i>Daily Prophet</i>, <a href="/wiki/1_September" title="1 September">1 September</a>, <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div><figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 160px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dp_severus_snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140531023911" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Dp severus snape"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Dp_severus_snape.jpg" 	data-image-name="Dp severus snape.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dp_severus_snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20140531023911"  	 width="160"  	 height="253"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dp_severus_snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20140531023911" 	 alt="Dp severus snape"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Dp_severus_snape.jpg" 	data-image-name="Dp severus snape.jpg" 	 	 width="160"  	 height="253"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dp_severus_snape.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i> reports Snape's appointment as Headmaster</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
</dd></dl>
<p>During the 1997-1998 school year, Snape was named Headmaster of Hogwarts, while Death Eaters <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto</a> and <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus Carrow</a> were appointed Deputy Heads. Snape used his position as Headmaster to discreetly protect the students and to contain the Carrows. It is later understood that, during his time as Headmaster, Snape consulted with the <a href="/wiki/Portrait" title="Portrait">portraits</a> of the previous <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmasters</a>, and continued to receive instructions from Dumbledore's portrait.
</p><p>Before the beginning of the first term, <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Scrimgeour" title="Rufus Scrimgeour">Rufus Scrimgeour</a> removed the Sword of Gryffindor from its glass case in the headmaster's office for examination, along with the other items Dumbledore left in his <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_will" title="Albus Dumbledore's will" class="mw-redirect">will</a>. However, this sword was a fake. The real sword had been hidden in a hole in the wall behind Dumbledore's portrait.
</p><p>When its counterfeit had been returned to Dumbledore's office, another attempt to seize the sword was made by <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>. After pretending to punish them by sending them into the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> with <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, Snape passed the fake sword along to <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, who kept it in her vault at <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts</a>, thinking that it was real.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 245px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Tumblr_mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3_250.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140621022650" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Tumblr mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3 250"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Tumblr_mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3_250.gif" 	data-image-name="Tumblr mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3 250.gif" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Tumblr_mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3_250.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140621022650"  	 width="245"  	 height="125"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Tumblr_mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3_250.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140621022650" 	 alt="Tumblr mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3 250"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Tumblr_mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3_250.gif" 	data-image-name="Tumblr mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3 250.gif" 	 	 width="245"  	 height="125"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tumblr_mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3_250.gif" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry being led by a doe Patronus (Snape's Patronus) to the hiding place of the <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" title="Godric Gryffindor's Sword" class="mw-redirect">Sword of Gryffindor</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Upon being informed by the portrait of <a href="/wiki/Phineas_Nigellus_Black" title="Phineas Nigellus Black">Phineas Nigellus Black</a> of Harry Potter's whereabouts, Dumbledore's portrait instructed Snape to give Harry the real sword without the latter knowing it. Not only would Harry not have taken kindly to Snape's appearance after his attack on <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a>, and also for the murder of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> of which Harry was an eye-witness, it would have been dangerous if Voldemort were to read his mind and see Snape helping him. Snape then took the real sword, hid it in a frozen pool of water near Harry's camping spot, and used his <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> to guide Harry to it. After having rescued Harry from drowning, Ron claimed to have supposedly seen someone watching from the shadows. Though not stated, it is extremely likely to have been Snape keeping an eye on Harry and only departing once he knew the latter was safe.
</p><p>As a headmaster, Snape was thoroughly disliked by many of his students. The old members of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore's Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> reformed the organisation after <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> gained control over the school and started up a revolt against Snape and the Carrows. Neville Longbottom, Luna Lovegood, and Ginny Weasley were at the forefront of the rebellion. Snape, following up on his promise to Dumbledore to keep the students safe, subtly undermined the violent, sadistic attempts of the Carrows to keep control by doing things such as sending students to help <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a> as punishments rather than the Carrows' more dangerous alternatives. Neville stated that Snape was hardly ever seen whilst headmaster. This could be because Snape remained in the headmaster's office most of the time or was searching for/following the trio to make sure they were safe and/or making progress. Also, during his tenure, the <a href="/wiki/Educational_Decree_Number_Twenty-Four" title="Educational Decree Number Twenty-Four">Educational Decree Number Twenty-Four</a> was re-enacted and students had taken to (most likely under Snape's orders) marching from point A to point B together like they were in military school.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Dismissal_as_Headmaster">Dismissal as Headmaster</span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>No! You'll do no more murder at Hogwarts!</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Filius Flitwick confronting Snape during his <a href="/wiki/Ousting_of_Severus_Snape" title="Ousting of Severus Snape">ousting</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div><figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif/revision/latest?cb=20110716140837" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Fiery Offensive Spell"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif" 	data-image-name="Fiery Offensive Spell.gif" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110716140837"  	 width="250"  	 height="103"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110716140837" 	 alt="Fiery Offensive Spell"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif" 	data-image-name="Fiery Offensive Spell.gif" 	 	 width="250"  	 height="103"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape duelling McGonagall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
</dd></dl>
<p>Harry, Ron, and Hermione returned to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Castle" title="Hogwarts Castle">Hogwarts Castle</a> in search of one of the last of Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, which they believed to have something to do with <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw" title="Rowena Ravenclaw">Rowena Ravenclaw</a>. The only idea they could come up with was <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw%27s_diadem" title="Rowena Ravenclaw's diadem" class="mw-redirect">Ravenclaw's lost diadem</a>, and so Harry and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> went to the <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw_Tower" title="Ravenclaw Tower">Ravenclaw Common Room</a> to get an idea of what the diadem looked like. Here they were met by <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto Carrow</a>, who pressed her finger to the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark" title="Dark Mark">Dark Mark</a> and summoned Voldemort.<sup id="cite_ref-DH29_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH29-28">[29]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus Carrow</a> arrived, but so did <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, and Snape subtly allowed the inept Death Eater Carrow siblings to be knocked out in the battle. As McGonagall rushed to meet with the other Heads of Houses to protect the school from Voldemort's oncoming attack, she was stopped by Snape, who demanded she tell him if she knew the whereabouts of Harry Potter.<sup id="cite_ref-DH30_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH30-29">[30]</a></sup>
</p><p>The two began fighting, and while Snape put up a good defence, McGonagall was soon helped by the arrival of the other Heads of House: <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Sprout</a>, <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Flitwick</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Slughorn</a>. Outnumbered, Snape fled the castle, jumping out the window of a classroom and using the ability to <a href="/wiki/Unsupported_flight" title="Unsupported flight">fly without a broom</a>, which he presumably learned from Voldemort.<sup id="cite_ref-DH30_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH30-29">[30]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_Hogwarts_and_death"><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> and death</span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>The Elder Wand cannot serve me properly, Severus, because I am not its true master. The Elder Wand belongs to the wizard who killed its last owner. You killed Albus Dumbledore. While you live, Severus, the Elder Wand cannot be truly mine</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Voldemort, explaining to Snape why he must murder him<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div><figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest?cb=20161218210623" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="B7C32M1 Nagini&amp;#039;s attack on Snape"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png" 	data-image-name="B7C32M1 Nagini&#39;s attack on Snape.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161218210623"  	 width="250"  	 height="98"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161218210623" 	 alt="B7C32M1 Nagini&amp;#039;s attack on Snape"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png" 	data-image-name="B7C32M1 Nagini&#39;s attack on Snape.png" 	 	 width="250"  	 height="98"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Nagini injects the venom into Snape's neck, killing him</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
</dd></dl>
<p>Later in the evening, Snape was summoned by Voldemort to the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a>. Voldemort explained that he believed that Snape was the master of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a> from killing Dumbledore and that Snape must die so that the Elder Wand can be his. Snape tried to explain the situation but Voldemort ordered <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a> to kill Snape by biting into his neck, injecting him with her extremely <a href="/wiki/Poison" title="Poison">poisonous</a> <a href="/wiki/Nagini%27s_venom" title="Nagini's venom">venom</a>, before he could finish speaking. Before dying, Snape released a cloud of memories and told Harry, who had watched the entire scene from a hidden spot, to take them.<sup id="cite_ref-DH32_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH32-30">[31]</a></sup> Harry later took the memories to the <a href="/wiki/Pensieve" title="Pensieve">Pensieve</a> in Dumbledore's office. From these memories, Harry learned everything about Snape's past. In the first scene, Harry discovered that Snape had befriended Lily as a nine-year-old child when they lived near each other in the industrial town of <a href="/wiki/Cokeworth" title="Cokeworth">Cokeworth</a>.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 236px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/DH2_memory_Lily_Evans_Sorted.gif/revision/latest?cb=20160822050346" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="DH2 memory Lily Evans Sorted"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="DH2_memory_Lily_Evans_Sorted.gif" 	data-image-name="DH2 memory Lily Evans Sorted.gif" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/DH2_memory_Lily_Evans_Sorted.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20160822050346"  	 width="236"  	 height="133"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/DH2_memory_Lily_Evans_Sorted.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20160822050346" 	 alt="DH2 memory Lily Evans Sorted"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="DH2_memory_Lily_Evans_Sorted.gif" 	data-image-name="DH2 memory Lily Evans Sorted.gif" 	 	 width="236"  	 height="133"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH2_memory_Lily_Evans_Sorted.gif" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape's memory of Lily being Sorted into Gryffindor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Upon their arrival at Hogwarts, the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sorting Hat</a> placed Snape and Lily into <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor Houses</a>, respectively. They remained close friends for the next few years until they were driven apart by Snape's interest in the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a> and by Lily's interest in <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>. The friendship finally ended following the incident that Harry had briefly witnessed in his fifth year, in which Snape accidentally insulted Lily. Despite this separation, and Snape's enmity toward Lily's eventual husband James Potter, Snape continued to love Lily on a much deeper and stronger romantic level for the rest of his life.
</p><p>Snape was next seen going to Dumbledore and desperately begging him to hide the Potters from Lord Voldemort, who was planning on targeting Lily's son to prevent <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney's first prophecy">a prophecy</a> from being fulfilled. Snape had been the one who previously revealed said prophecy to Voldemort, not knowing at first that it was referring to Lily and her family. Though he asked Voldemort to spare Lily, Snape still feared for her safety, as he knew that Voldemort could not be relied on to grant this small favour. Snape became a double agent for the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> so that Dumbledore could ensure Lily's protection, employing <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> to hide his duplicity from his master.
</p><p>Snape felt devastating pain and remorse when Lily was found and murdered. From that point on, he agreed to help Dumbledore protect her son and fight against Lord Voldemort. Snape demanded, however, that his feelings about Lily be kept a secret. Dumbledore complied and never told anyone the real reason why Snape switched sides.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/49/Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811020304" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Albus Dumbledore wearing Marvolo Gaunt&amp;#039;s Ring"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg" 	data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore wearing Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s Ring.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/49/Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180811020304"  	 width="250"  	 height="104"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/49/Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180811020304" 	 alt="Albus Dumbledore wearing Marvolo Gaunt&amp;#039;s Ring"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg" 	data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore wearing Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s Ring.jpg" 	 	 width="250"  	 height="104"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marvolo Gaunt's ring with a curse that was slowly killing Dumbledore</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape's memories then revealed that Severus slowed the spread of the curse afflicted on Dumbledore, after he put Marvolo Gaunt's ring. However, the curse would have ultimately killed Albus within a year. Dumbledore, knowing that Draco Malfoy was ordered by Voldemort to kill him, and expecting the boy will fail, asked Snape to kill himself instead of Draco in order to gain Voldemort's complete trust and learn more of his plans.
</p><p>At the end Snape's memories showed Snape's outrage after learning that Harry had to die. Snape ultimately revealed his Patronus, a doe, the same as Lily's, showing he still, after all these years, loved her.
</p><p>Because of the memories, Harry finally understood where Snape's true allegiances always were. The memories provided Harry with the information he needed to ensure Voldemort's final defeat. He also showed Harry the memory where Albus Dumbledore had told him about Harry himself being a <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a> (although he did not understand it) because Dumbledore had asked him to pass that along to Harry when the time was right.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-mortem">Post-mortem</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Severus Snape wasn't yours, Snape was Dumbledore's, Dumbledore's from the moment you started hunting down my mother!... He was Dumbledore's spy from the moment you threatened her, and he's been working against you ever since!</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Harry reveals Snape's true colours during the final duel<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div><figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest?cb=20150904231059" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="B7C36M2 Voldemort vanquished"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" 	data-image-name="B7C36M2 Voldemort vanquished.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059"  	 width="250"  	 height="97"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" 	 alt="B7C36M2 Voldemort vanquished"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" 	data-image-name="B7C36M2 Voldemort vanquished.png" 	 	 width="250"  	 height="97"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The final duel between <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and Lord Voldemort</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
</dd></dl>
<p>During the final duel between Harry and <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>, Harry finally told him that Snape had been, in fact, Dumbledore's man. Harry also revealed that Snape was never the true master of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a>, because Snape never defeated Dumbledore; the two had arranged his death as he would have died either way. Before Snape killed Dumbledore, <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">disarmed</a> Dumbledore. Therefore, Draco was the true master of the Elder Wand, not Snape. However, Harry had overpowered Draco at Malfoy Manor and taken his wand. Because of the subtleties governing wand ownership discussed by <a href="/wiki/Garrick_Ollivander" title="Garrick Ollivander">Garrick Ollivander</a>, Harry was the current master of the Elder Wand. Snape's true loyalties remained hidden due to his skills as an <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumens</a> and the fact his actions were motivated by love, which completely eluded Voldemort.
</p><p>Snape's <a href="/wiki/Portrait" title="Portrait">portrait</a> was not automatically put into the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_office" title="Headmaster's office" class="mw-redirect">Headmaster's office</a> since he had essentially abandoned his post during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. However, Harry, in one of his acts of showing reconciliation towards Snape, made sure that his portrait was placed there.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">[32]</a></sup> It is possible that Harry gave his corpse a proper burial after the war ended. <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> also published a book about Snape's life, entitled <i><a href="/wiki/Snape:_Scoundrel_or_Saint%3F" title="Snape: Scoundrel or Saint?">Snape: Scoundrel or Saint?</a></i>, sometime after his death.<sup id="cite_ref-bloomsbury-20070730_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bloomsbury-20070730-32">[33]</a></sup> If it is consistent with Skeeter's other works, it is probably riddled with inaccuracies designed to tarnish Snape's reputation.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus Potter</a>, the second son of Harry, and the only one of Harry's children to have inherited Lily's bright green almond-shaped eyes, is named after Snape. When Albus was worried that he may be Sorted into Slytherin, Harry responded that Albus was named after two headmasters, one of whom was a <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> and "<i>probably the bravest man I ever knew</i>".
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternate_timeline">Alternate timeline</span></h3>
<p>By his fourth year at Hogwarts, <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a> had learned all about Snape's history and motivations, allowing him to convince an alternate version of Snape — in a timeline where Voldemort won the Battle of Hogwarts and thus ruled wizarding Britain — that he came from a different timeline so that Snape could help Scorpius meet the local resistance and undo what he had unwittingly done to the past. This version of Snape correctly guessed that he had died in the struggle against Voldemort in Scorpius' timeline but proceeded to aid him nonetheless. After <a href="/wiki/Banishing_Charm" title="Banishing Charm">knocking down</a> <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> to allow <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a> to escape, he was attacked by the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a>, leaving his fate unknown.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">[34]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_appearance">Physical appearance</span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span>"<i>...he most likely valued other qualities within himself.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> on why Snape was so poorly groomed<sup id="cite_ref-bloomsbury-20070730_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bloomsbury-20070730-32">[33]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 156px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/SnapeHBP.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20120222145646" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="SnapeHBP"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="SnapeHBP.JPG" 	data-image-name="SnapeHBP.JPG" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/SnapeHBP.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20120222145646"  	 width="156"  	 height="240"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/SnapeHBP.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20120222145646" 	 alt="SnapeHBP"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="SnapeHBP.JPG" 	data-image-name="SnapeHBP.JPG" 	 	 width="156"  	 height="240"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:SnapeHBP.JPG" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Severus Snape</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Severus Snape was a thin man with sallow skin, a large, hooked nose and yellow, uneven teeth. He usually dressed in flowing black robes which made him resemble "<i>an overgrown bat</i>". He had shoulder-length, greasy black hair which framed his face in curtains, curling lips and dark, penetrating eyes that resembled tunnels. As a Death Eater, he bore the Dark Mark on his left inner forearm.
</p><p>The younger Snape had a "<i>stringy, pallid look</i>", being "<i>round-shouldered yet angular</i>" and with a "<i>twitchy walk that recalled a spider</i>", as well as "<i>long oily hair that jumped about his face</i>."
</p><p>Snape had a strong, authoritative presence. He spoke in a soft, contained voice most of the time, except during the occasional instances when he lost his temper.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality_and_traits">Personality and traits</span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Don't push it. I've heard Snape can turn very nasty.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Snape's infamous temper described by Ronald Weasley<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
