<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 232px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/Potion_Class.png/revision/latest?cb=20131027180649" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Potion Class"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Potion_Class.png" 	data-image-name="Potion Class.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/Potion_Class.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/232?cb=20131027180649"  	 width="232"  	 height="96"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/Potion_Class.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/232?cb=20131027180649" 	 alt="Potion Class"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Potion_Class.png" 	data-image-name="Potion Class.png" 	 	 width="232"  	 height="96"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Potion_Class.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">His first potion class with Harry and the rest of the students, where he lecturers Harry in front of the class for "not paying attention" when he was taking notes</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170721221152" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Order-of-the-phoenix-snape"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg" 	data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170721221152"  	 width="180"  	 height="75"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170721221152" 	 alt="Order-of-the-phoenix-snape"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg" 	data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="75"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape slapping Ron Weasley over the head with a book for laughing</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
A complicated, withdrawn person, Severus Snape's life was overwhelmed with many complex emotions that he never fully disclosed. At times, Snape could appear cold, cynical, malicious, bitter, and sarcastic. He had a commanding presence that exuded gravitas, authority and control; like <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professor McGonagall</a>, he had the ability to keep a class quiet without effort. He tended to hold grudges and was extremely spiteful toward those whom he disliked. In particular, he disdained <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> students, considering them to be arrogant and attention-seeking. Descriptions of his social interactions as a child suggest that he had poor interpersonal skills and that he may have suffered from depression. <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 235px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20160822105257" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="SnapeHarryRonClass"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG" 	data-image-name="SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20160822105257"  	 width="235"  	 height="156"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20160822105257" 	 alt="SnapeHarryRonClass"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG" 	data-image-name="SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG" 	 	 width="235"  	 height="156"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape's brand of class discipline toward Gryffindors</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>Snape was a repressed, solitary man with no friends. In his early life, he was insecure, vulnerable, and yearned to be part of something better. As a child, the bleak normality of working-class suburbia compounded with his neglectful <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> <a href="/wiki/Tobias_Snape" title="Tobias Snape">father</a> inspired in him a contempt for ordinariness. This urgent desire to be a part of something powerful and important was what drew him to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">inner circle</a>. Snape's bitterness and resentment towards the world was exacerbated even more by the relentless bullying he endured in school, causing him to shut himself in even more. Snape was not a prejudiced individual despite the Death Eater beliefs of pure-blood superiority, but was rather against Muggles, presumably because of his sour experience with both his father and Petunia Evans, but held no ill-will towards <a href="/wiki/Muggle-borns" title="Muggle-borns" class="mw-redirect">Muggle-borns</a>. The foundation of him scolding Lily Evans by calling her Mudblood was to not appear weak in front of his fellow Death Eater students than actual supremacist views. He also deeply regretted this as it was what ended his friendship with Lily and defended Hermione Granger when <a href="/wiki/Phineas_Nigellus_Black" title="Phineas Nigellus Black">Phineas Nigellus Black</a> called her Mudblood, his manner of speaking in this instance being uncharacteristically explosive and filled with more emotion than he normally displayed.
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Fools who wear their hearts proudly on their sleeves, who cannot control their emotions, who wallow in sad memories and allow themselves to be provoked this easily — weak people, in other words — they stand no chance against his powers!</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Snape's opinion on emotionalism and self-control<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div><figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 241px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Snape%26harry.gif/revision/latest?cb=20141009143617" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Snape&amp;amp;harry"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Snape%26harry.gif" 	data-image-name="Snape&amp;amp;harry.gif" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Snape%26harry.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20141009143617"  	 width="241"  	 height="118"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Snape%26harry.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20141009143617" 	 alt="Snape&amp;amp;harry"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Snape%26harry.gif" 	data-image-name="Snape&amp;amp;harry.gif" 	 	 width="241"  	 height="118"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape%26harry.gif" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape threatens Harry after an Occlumency lesson</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
</dd></dl>
<p>He was an intensely private individual who viewed emotional displays as a sign of shameful weakness. As an <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumens</a>, Snape had superb emotional control and was adept at concealing his thoughts and feelings, which allowed him to maintain his cold, collected demeanour. However, he had his limits, and was not incapable of losing his temper, particularly when it came to dealing with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>. Inevitably, he also became furious when he thought he was being pitied or accused of cowardice.
</p><p>Snape was a formidable sorcerer, displaying consummate skill in many different branches of <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magic</a>. His extensive knowledge and abilities were rivalled by very few, if any other <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witches and wizards</a> of his age. Snape was also unusually cerebral for a <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a>, possessing a subtle and keenly analytical mind. As a result, Snape was extremely intelligent and calculative, with a mind for strategy and deduction. He was also a profound misanthrope who appeared to have a prominent hatred of almost every child under his tutelage, except of course for <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherins</a>. He valued logic and cunning above magical power.
</p><p>As a professor, Snape was known for his cavalier and harshly authoritarian attitude towards his teaching. His standards for his classes were much higher than that of the other professors, as he only allowed students with the very best grades to continue into advanced study. As Potions Master, he described it as an art and an exact science, and dismissed the use of incantations and wand waving as "silly and foolish". He developed a loving passion for Dark Arts, originally in the hopes to cover the shame of his heritage, and his interest in it led him to repeatedly apply for the Defence Against the Dark Arts professor post every year, despite being rejected for sixteen years. He knew full well why Dumbledore never granted him the position, as it may be a trigger to bring out his worst side, something he denied to Umbridge's questioning but let in to those of Bellatrix's. When he finally got his wish, Snape taught the course with a loving caress in his voice, far beyond simply respecting the Dark Arts as a dangerous foe, something he did not show in his post as the Potions Master. He also taught this class slightly fairer than he did in Potions, such as lowering his entrance standards and biases for <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T. level</a> classes, allowing more students to enter the advanced studies of his favourite class, and placed students from his own house, such as <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Vincent Crabbe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Gregory Goyle</a>, in detention for failing to do acceptable work the second time around after failing their <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> the previous year.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 251px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/Snape%27sPatronus.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20111111161715" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Snape&amp;#039;sPatronus"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Snape%27sPatronus.JPG" 	data-image-name="Snape&#39;sPatronus.JPG" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/Snape%27sPatronus.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20111111161715"  	 width="251"  	 height="103"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/Snape%27sPatronus.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20111111161715" 	 alt="Snape&amp;#039;sPatronus"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Snape%27sPatronus.JPG" 	data-image-name="Snape&#39;sPatronus.JPG" 	 	 width="251"  	 height="103"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape%27sPatronus.JPG" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape showing Dumbledore his true and undying love for <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ultimately, it was Snape's past and his love for Lily Evans that defined his inner being. His love for Lily Evans became most noticeable by his Patronus; a Doe, just like Lily's. Upon overhearing <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney's first prophecy">the Prophecy</a>, he immediately informed his then-master of its contents, unaware that this would endanger Lily and her family. It was only after <a href="/wiki/Attack_at_Godric%27s_Hollow_(1981)" title="Attack at Godric's Hollow (1981)">Lily's death</a> that Snape realised the full extent of his actions. He suffered terrible remorse for what he had done and spent the rest of his life in constant danger in order to protect Lily's son.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>You are a braver man by far than Igor Karkaroff. You know, I sometimes think we <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sort</a> too soon...</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Snape's bravery despite the dangers to his own life<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<p>In spite of his vindictive demeanour, Severus Snape was an immensely brave man who possessed a deep capacity for <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a>. Everything that he did in the latter part of his life was motivated by his devotion to Lily Evans, whom he loved unconditionally. He was one of Dumbledore's most reliable allies and in his role as a double agent, took great personal risk in ensuring Harry's safety from Lord Voldemort. Despite his years of him and Harry barely getting along, if at all, Snape openly criticised Dumbledore after learning he protected Harry all these years just so he could die at the right time due to being a Horcrux, showing he didn't agree with Harry's death even though, at first, he only protected him because of his relationship to Lily. When he informed Dumbledore that he informed Voldemort of the prophecy, Snape begged Dumbledore to hide Harry, Lily, and even James too. This clearly showed that Snape prioritised Lily's happiness above all else, even if it meant her being with a man he hated for most of his life. 
</p><p>Despite his coldness towards all but Lily, Snape nevertheless proved capable of genuinely caring for others apart from Lily and Harry. He showed that despite his mistreatment of them, he cared considerably for the students of Hogwarts, risking his façade for them by secretly doing everything he can to make sure they stayed out of harms way and at one point being genuinely concerned when a student was taken to the Chamber of Secrets. Additionally, Snape was also genuinely saddened by the death of Rowan Khanna, his face just as mournful as the rest of the other House Heads, and if Rowan were in Slytherin, Snape even went as far as to plead with Merula to stop being angry and comfort them with the prospect of standing together in the face of crisis. While he initially resented Dumbledore for his lack of intervention on his torturous bullying by the Marauders, it seemed the time he spent allying with Dumbledore had made him grow to genuinely as well as greatly respect and even care for him, as shown by how he was clearly shocked into being silent for a long time after Dumbledore asked Snape to kill him, clearly indicated that killing Dumbledore was hard for him to do and tried to make him have Draco kill him instead of having Snape do it. Even after learning of how Dumbledore had wanted Harry to die so Voldemort can be defeated, when preparing to kill Dumbledore, his face was described as being genuinely hateful and disgusted of what he was about to do.
</p><p>Despite Snape's normally calm and controlled exterior and guarded body language, he was in possession of an extraordinarily explosive and almost psychotic temper. This was rarely seen, but an extreme display of rage was most prominently witnessed after Snape killed Dumbledore and was confronted outside of Hagrid's burning house near the edge of the school grounds. The event that triggered this unhinged manifestation of Snape's unrestrained wrath was Harry's accusation of Snape being a coward for killing Dumbledore.
</p><p>Due to the many years of being bullied by Harry's father, and with a need to both vent his immense stress and maintain his cover as a loyal <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a>, Snape unleashed a terrifying mix of both his emotions and magic in his duel with Harry, taking great pleasure in torturing and punishing the son of his enemy. Unlike in the past where he spoke quietly in his anger, Snape in this instance was screaming and letting so much out, as well as confessing his identity of the Half-Blood Prince to Harry who had attempted to use one of Snape's own invented spells against him. This battle showed Snape's repressed rage in its horrific glory and power. Suffice it to say, Severus Snape was not a man who it was wise to provoke, lest one incur his almost elemental wrath and magical power.  
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Magical_abilities_and_skills">Magical abilities and skills</span></h2>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 240px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/Tumblr_n63uvuK3FL1ruo0fko10_r1_250.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140619155902" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Tumblr n63uvuK3FL1ruo0fko10 r1 250"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Tumblr_n63uvuK3FL1ruo0fko10_r1_250.gif" 	data-image-name="Tumblr n63uvuK3FL1ruo0fko10 r1 250.gif" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/Tumblr_n63uvuK3FL1ruo0fko10_r1_250.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20140619155902"  	 width="240"  	 height="129"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/Tumblr_n63uvuK3FL1ruo0fko10_r1_250.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20140619155902" 	 alt="Tumblr n63uvuK3FL1ruo0fko10 r1 250"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Tumblr_n63uvuK3FL1ruo0fko10_r1_250.gif" 	data-image-name="Tumblr n63uvuK3FL1ruo0fko10 r1 250.gif" 	 	 width="240"  	 height="129"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tumblr_n63uvuK3FL1ruo0fko10_r1_250.gif" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Severus Snape's corporeal <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> (the form of a doe)</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>Snape knew more curses when he arrived at Hogwarts than half the kids in seventh year.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Snape's proficiency for the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<p>Severus Snape was an extremely powerful and skilled <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a>, showing proficient talent and great knowledge in many different areas of magic. He had an encyclopaedic knowledge and proficiency in potions, was incredibly talented in <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimency</a> and <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a>, and was also the only <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> capable of producing a Patronus.
</p>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">Magical</a> mastery</b>: Even at a young age, Severus was a gifted wizard, having knowledge of deep secrets of the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a> that he would usually relay to his crush, <a href="/wiki/Lily_Potter" title="Lily Potter">Lily Potter</a>. In addition, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, a known rival of his, claimed that Severus knew more about the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a> than half of the seventh year's at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, which speaks for his seemingly encyclopaedic knowledge of magic. He was proficient in creating many useful spells used by the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> and even his rivals. He was also proficient in altering the formula for potions, resulting in an easier and more efficient way to produce them, which enhanced <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>'s proficiency in Potions to the point of easily surpassing even the results of Hermione Granger. His magical prowess was so great as a teenager that his bully and rival, <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a> would never have taken him on in a one on one fight unless he was backed up by his three other <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">talented friends</a>. As an adult, Snape had became an incredibly powerful and skilled wizard and acknowledged by his fellow professors and <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> for his great prowess. He proved capable of effortlessly defeating the likes of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and also holding his own against the extremely powerful witch <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, who was capable of surviving a duel with Voldemort himself.
</li><li><b><a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">Love</a></b>: Severus was one of the only people in Voldemort's inner circle who was capable of feeling unconditional love. He fell deeply in love with <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> as a child and maintained his devotion to her until his death. Despite their differences in beliefs about many things, Severus felt nothing but absolute love for Lily even though she never extended her reciprocity beyond friendship. Snape was devastated by Lily's death and expressed suicidal desires. However, so great was his love, he forced his way past them and spent seventeen years in constant danger in order to protect Lily's son and ensure that her sacrifice was not in vain. Indeed, Snape's <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> was a doe, just like Lily's, showing that his love for her was far stronger than his loyalty to Lord Voldemort. Due to this, Snape was the only <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> who was able to cast a Patronus. Furthermore, his insight into the nature of love was evident when teaching <a href="/wiki/Love_Potion" title="Love Potion">Love Potions</a>, as he was able to distinguish between the obsessive love caused by love potions and the genuine, unconditional love that most people felt for each other.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">[35]</a></sup>
</li><li><b><a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a></b>: Severus had a passion for the Dark Arts from a young age, and was especially talented with <a href="/wiki/Curse" title="Curse">curses</a>, or so some believed. According to Sirius Black, Snape was "<i>up to his eyeballs in the Dark Arts</i>" when he was at school. However, they had an age old rivalry which could have influenced Sirius's words. When he was still a student, Snape was already talented enough that he was capable of creating new dark spells, as most of the spells he created were curses, <a href="/wiki/Hex" title="Hex">hexes</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Jinx" title="Jinx">jinxes</a>. As an adult at least, Snape was capable of performing the <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a>, one of the <a href="/wiki/Unforgivable_Curses" title="Unforgivable Curses">Unforgivable Curses</a> that required a considerable level of magical skill, using the curse to kill Dumbledore on his orders. 
</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">"<i>Time to stir my <a href="/wiki/Cauldron" title="Cauldron">cauldron</a>. I bet Snape could do this with his eyes closed.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Jacob's sibling<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Hogwarts_Mystery" title="Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">Potions</a></b>: Severus was extremely adept in the art of potion-making and worked as the <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a> at Hogwarts for about fifteen years. His prowess at potion-making extended beyond simple execution from formally documented recipes accepted and followed by the general public. When he was still only a student, he would alter official instructions with his own variations, which usually resulted in quicker and more efficient results. He was capable of brewing highly complicated potions such as <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wolfsbane_Potion" title="Wolfsbane Potion">Wolfsbane Potion</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Mandrake_Restorative_Draught" title="Mandrake Restorative Draught">Mandrake Restorative Draught</a>. Snape was also able to identify <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> by smell and produce fake Veritaserum that seemed real enough to fool Dolores Umbridge (though Umbridge was not portrayed as being particularly intelligent with practicality). In addition, Snape used an <a href="/wiki/Thick_golden_potion" title="Thick golden potion">unidentified golden potion</a> to help slow a <a href="/wiki/Curse_on_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_ring" title="Curse on Marvolo Gaunt's ring">curse</a> that was slowly killing Dumbledore.
</li><li><b><a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a></b>: Though Snape had a zest for dark magic, he possessed outstanding knowledge and abilities in protecting from it. His encyclopaedic understanding of the dark arts may have contributed to this. Snape taught the class at N.E.W.T level to such an effect that even Harry Potter could not help but be enchanted by his knowledge. Snape effectively "assisted" the 1992 duelling club, and understood the need for students handling pragmatism as well as theory in the subject. Snape's speciality in DADA was particularly in the area of counter-curses. In fact, his abilities in countering curses were so great that he was able to temporarily save Dumbledore (himself an expert on the subject) with wand enhanced incantations and a <a href="/wiki/Thick_golden_potion" title="Thick golden potion">potion</a> simultaneously from a "<i>curse of extraordinary power</i>", Dumbledore noted that he was only able to (temporarily) survive due to Snape's expertise. He was also able to prevent the curse that Katie Bell was inflicted with when she touched the necklace on Borgin and Burkes from spreading any further, saving her life. Snape had also developed effective counter curses for his own dark spells, such as the magic he used to heal Draco from the effects of <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i>.
</li><li><b><a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> and <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimency</a></b>: Snape's unerring ability to conceal his thoughts and feelings from external penetration proved to be crucial for him. His skills in Occlumency was so great that for seventeen years, he managed to hide facts from <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> such as his remorse for Lily Evans's death and his secret alliance with Albus Dumbledore; it was his mastery of hiding his mind that made both sides distrust him. Snape was also very skilled at Legilimency; Harry Potter often felt as if Snape had the ability to read minds even before learning what the art was. Snape used Legilimency on Harry constantly, while attempting to teach him Occlumency in their private lessons and later used it to effortlessly deflect Harry's spells and curses. Despite his skill in Legilimency he was may have been unable to read <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>'s thoughts when the latter was a relatively inexperienced Occlumens (though Draco may have only believed that he was able to block Snape). Since Voldemort was considered history's greatest legilimens and was unable to ever read Snape's mind, despite being in the same room with him on many occasions, Snape could be history's greatest occlumens, with the possible exception of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>, both of whom proved able to also deflect Voldemort's Legilimency. Considering how Voldemort would have detected Snape resisting penetration, Snape would've had to be careful only to block certain thoughts from him while allowing Voldemort to only see what would reinforce his belief in Snape's loyalty.
</li><li><b><a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a></b>: Severus was highly accomplished with transfiguration, given his proficiency with <a href="/wiki/Conjuration" title="Conjuration">Conjuration</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vanishment" title="Vanishment">Vanishment</a>, two very difficult and advanced branches of this field. He was talented with the vanishing of physical matter, as shown when he vanished Harry Potter's failed <a href="/wiki/Draught_of_Peace" title="Draught of Peace">Draught of Peace</a> potion in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Vanishing_Spell" title="Vanishing Spell">Vanishing Spell</a><sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_27-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-27">[28]</a></sup> and when he vanished the <a href="/wiki/Snake" title="Snake">snake</a> that <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> <a href="/wiki/Snake_Summons_Spell" title="Snake Summons Spell">summoned</a> in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Snake-Vanishing_Spell" title="Snake-Vanishing Spell">Snake-Vanishing Spell</a>. He also successfully conjured ropes with the <a href="/wiki/Incarcerous_Spell" title="Incarcerous Spell">Incarcerous Spell</a> to bind <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> and <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a> in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>. He also transfigured the whirlwind-shaped fire that McGonagall launched at him shortly before the Battle of Hogwarts into a great black snake.
</li><li><b><a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a></b>: Snape was highly talented in charms as he not only could use basic to advanced charms without fail, such as <a href="/wiki/Levitation" title="Levitation">levitation</a>, <a href="/wiki/Disarming_charm" title="Disarming charm" class="mw-redirect">disarming</a>, <a href="/wiki/Summoning_Charm" title="Summoning Charm">summoning</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mending_Charm" title="Mending Charm">repairing</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wand-Lighting_Charm" title="Wand-Lighting Charm">illuminating</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fire-Making_Spell" title="Fire-Making Spell">igniting</a>, <a href="/wiki/Water-Making_Spell" title="Water-Making Spell">creating water</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shield_Charm" title="Shield Charm">shielding</a> and <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">stunning</a>, but he was even able to cast the incredibly difficult <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charm</a>, conjuring a corporeal doe Patronus. He was also able to <a href="/wiki/Blackboard_Writing_Spell" title="Blackboard Writing Spell">write instructions on a blackboard</a> with a single flick of his wand.
</li><li><b><a href="/wiki/Flight" title="Flight">Flying</a></b>: Snape was a very capable flyer on a <a href="/wiki/Broomstick" title="Broomstick">broomstick</a>, as during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, he was not blasted off his broom and knowledgeable enough in the rules of <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> to take over the position of referee at least once. However, in one of Snape's memories, Lily was laughing as he attempted to mount a bucking broomstick, so perhaps he was not always a good flyer. Later on, Severus was also capable of <a href="/wiki/Unsupported_flight" title="Unsupported flight">Unsupported flight</a>. The only other known wizard that was able to do this was Lord Voldemort himself (who is likely to have passed down this skill to Snape personally). In 1997, he used this skill to escape from Hogwarts after his duel with Minerva McGonagall.
</li></ul>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 154px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0d/SnapeDuelingClub.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160819104725" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="SnapeDuelingClub"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="SnapeDuelingClub.jpg" 	data-image-name="SnapeDuelingClub.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0d/SnapeDuelingClub.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20160819104725"  	 width="154"  	 height="233"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0d/SnapeDuelingClub.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20160819104725" 	 alt="SnapeDuelingClub"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="SnapeDuelingClub.jpg" 	data-image-name="SnapeDuelingClub.jpg" 	 	 width="154"  	 height="233"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:SnapeDuelingClub.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape in a duelling demonstration during the first meeting of the <a href="/wiki/Duelling_Club" title="Duelling Club">Duelling Club</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">Duelling</a></b>: Although he rarely engaged in duels, Snape was shown to be a highly capable duellist. During his days as a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> he likely had to fight against <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">aurors</a> and members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. He was able to hold his own against the extremely powerful <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> (who was capable of duelling Voldemort along with Kingsley and Slughorn) during their brief duel, before she forced him to hide behind a shield of armour. He then fled when <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Pomona Sprout</a> and <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a> arrived to assist He assisted in a duelling club in 1992 with <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>, effortlessly defeating him with a single spell, though, as Lockhart was an unskilled wizard, this was not such a great achievement. Snape also easily overwhelmed <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> during his escape from the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> and defeated him without much effort, using <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimency</a> to read Harry's attempted moves and countered them all before they could be cast. Severus participated in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, joining the Death Eaters's side (though secretly attempted to protect the Order), and survived unharmed. Contrary to the vicious duelling styles of other Death Eaters, Snape preferred using defensive spells and only used aggressive magic when facing a weak opponent, such as Lockhart, or when his foe grew frustrated and started making mistakes. Snape was never known to battle a Death Eater or ally to Voldemort (which would've blown his cover) but no Death Eater ever dared raise a wand against him (even the notoriously powerful <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>) and showed fear towards him, indicating they must have seen him display remarkable duelling skills.
</li><li><b><a href="/wiki/Spell_creation" title="Spell creation">Spell creation</a></b>: As a student at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, Severus was very inventive with new <a href="/wiki/Spell" title="Spell">spells</a>. Some of the spells he created were <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Langlock" title="Langlock">Langlock</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Muffliato_Charm" title="Muffliato Charm">Muffliato</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Levicorpus" title="Levicorpus">Levicorpus</a></i> and its <a href="/wiki/Counter-jinx" title="Counter-jinx">Counter-jinx</a> <i><a href="/wiki/Liberacorpus" title="Liberacorpus">Liberacorpus</a></i>. The last two somehow became common knowledge around the school. It is unknown what thoughts and techniques Snape put into his creations.
</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>BANG! Thin, snakelike cords brust from the end of Snape's wand and twisted themselves around Lupin's mouth, wrists, and ankles</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Snape <a href="/wiki/Conjuration" title="Conjuration">conjures</a> ropes non-verbally<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Wandless" title="Wandless">Wandless</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_spell" title="Nonverbal spell">nonverbal</a> magic</b>: Snape was highly skilled at using non-verbal spells, from the most basic uses (such as instruction-writing on blackboards and cleanups) to the most advanced (such as combat curses). Snape was also skilled at performing wandless magic, such as rope conjuring, counter-jinxing and memory extraction. (Although memory extraction does not require explicitly the use of a wand, relying instead on direct eye contact, conjuring and counter-jinxing are more often depicted to take place with the help of a wand.)
</li><li><b><a href="/wiki/Alchemy" title="Alchemy">Alchemy</a></b>: Intimately connected with <a href="/wiki/Potions" title="Potions" class="mw-redirect">potion-making</a> among other things, Snape had great respect for the field of alchemy, believing it was as much about gaining intellectual wealth as the physical one. Deeming it more advanced than his <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">usual lessons</a>, to the point where he initially asked <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob's sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> if the latter was joking when they asked whether he would be willing to teach alchemy to themselves and the visiting <a href="/wiki/Beauxbatons_Academy_of_Magic" title="Beauxbatons Academy of Magic">Beauxbatons</a> <a href="/wiki/Aur%C3%A9lie_Dumont" title="Aurélie Dumont">student</a>, insisting that he would only ever consider giving lessons on the subject to a select few of his very best students, such as <a href="/wiki/Penny_Haywood" title="Penny Haywood">Penny Haywood</a>. Displaying a fair amount of knowledge on the topic, he was able to host a private lesson and give <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob's sibling">Jacob's sibling</a>, <a href="/wiki/Penny_Haywood" title="Penny Haywood">Penny Haywood</a> and <a href="/wiki/Aur%C3%A9lie_Dumont" title="Aurélie Dumont">Aurélie Dumont</a> a lecture on the philosophy, history and teachings of the subject, as well as <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher's Stone">its objectives</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">[36]</a></sup>
</li><li><b><a href="/wiki/Healing_magic" title="Healing magic">Healing magic</a></b>: Snape was also very skilled with healing magic, as he reduced the effects of the <a href="/wiki/Curse_on_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_ring" title="Curse on Marvolo Gaunt's ring">Curse on Marvolo Gaunt's ring</a> on <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> which allowed him to survive for at least a year and saved <a href="/wiki/Katie_Bell" title="Katie Bell">Katie Bell</a>'s life by preventing any further spread of the <a href="/wiki/Opal_Necklace" title="Opal Necklace">cursed necklace</a> in her body. He also healed <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>'s wounds with <i><a href="/wiki/Vulnera_Sanentur" title="Vulnera Sanentur">Vulnera Sanentur</a>,</i> a <a href="/wiki/Healing_spell" title="Healing spell">healing spell</a> and <a href="/wiki/Counter-curse" title="Counter-curse">counter-curse</a>, after Harry Potter recklessly used the <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i> curse on him and seriously injured him. His knowledge in healing was such that Dumbledore once quoted to Harry that Snape was more experienced in healing against Dark magic than <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Poppy Pomfrey</a> was. He also successfully brewed the <a href="/wiki/Mandrake_Restorative_Draught" title="Mandrake Restorative Draught">Mandrake Restorative Draught</a> in the <a href="/wiki/1992%E2%80%931993_school_year" title="1992–1993 school year">1992–1993 school year</a>, which cured all the victims of <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">petrification</a> that year.
</li><li><b>Intellectual giftedness</b>: Snape's logic and deductive reasoning skills were such that he helped protect the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher's Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a> by creating an obstacle, which was based on logic rather than magical skill. According to <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, many powerful wizards have a blind spot in regards to logic.
</li><li><b>Teaching skills</b>: Despite his unpleasant nature and strained relationship with many of the Hogwarts students outside <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a>, Snape was nevertheless a relatively effective teacher as the <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a> and was one of the few teachers at Hogwarts who could keep a class quiet with minimal effort, with some students like <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> able to achieve <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.s</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.s</a> under his teaching, despite Snape only allowing students with top grades to do Potions in the NEWT level. His teaching skills were also effective enough for him to be respected by most of the other professors until he killed <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a>, pass <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>'s inspection of him and for <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> to make him <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> of Hogwarts. Additionally, while <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> did not learn much from Snape due to their mutual dislike of each other, the instructions Snape wrote in his <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_copy_of_Advanced_Potion-Making" title="Severus Snape's copy of Advanced Potion-Making">Copy of Advanced Potion-Making</a> were effective enough to make Harry improve his own performance in Potions in his sixth year, suggesting that Snape would have been more respected as a teacher if he was less unpleasant and used these instructions more.
</li><li><b>Acting skills</b>: Snape was an extremely adept actor, as he flawlessly succeeded in hiding his true allegiance to <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, even able to fool <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> himself completely to the point of the latter having complete trust in him to such an extent that after he killed Dumbledore, Voldemort was fully willing to make him Hogwart's <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a>. Snape's skill in acting allowed him to keep his motives dubious in the eyes of both friend and ally alike. This makes Snape likely the most accomplished actor and spy in wizarding history.
</li><li><b>Poetry</b>: A skill that Snape possessed but did not make very much mention or display of, Snape was capable of fluidly crafting his words in a way that could often befuddle the reader. His only known composition was the logic puzzle that he used as part of his defences of the Philosopher's Stone. Since this poem showed Snape's logical thinking, it was obviously one of his own creation. Snape's other possible works, if they exist, remain unknown.
</li><li><b>Indomitable willpower</b>: Snape, despite his personal demons, possessed immense willpower and bravery, being a respected hero of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a> and having great respect from both <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> (the latter of whom would go so far as to declare Snape to be "the bravest man [he] ever knew"). Hence, despite his great love for <a href="/wiki/Lily_Potter" title="Lily Potter">Lily Potter</a> and being aware of her intense disapproval for the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a>, Snape refused to relinquish his interest for the practice nor abandon the approval of his <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> friends for her. Later, while guilt-ridden and devastated, feeling personally responsible for Lily's death, Snape refused to succumb to despair and instead dedicated himself to honouring Lily in death by working closely with Dumbledore to protect Harry and ensure that her sacrifice was not in vain. As such, despite the extremely dangerous and seemingly impossible task of bringing down the most powerful <a href="/wiki/Dark_wizard" title="Dark wizard" class="mw-redirect">Dark wizard</a> of all time, <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, Snape refused to back down from it and resolved to faithfully execute Dumbledore's many complex and intricate plans to bring down the Dark Lord, with him valiantly working as an undercover agent for the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> for sixteen years and steadfastly spying on the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, with this ultimately ensuring Voldemort's defeat at the hands of Harry. Snape's willpower and determination also allowed him to persistently apply for the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> post for fifteen years (despite Dumbledore repeatedly refusing him the job) and to completely master the notably difficult skills of <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> and <a href="/wiki/Non-verbal_magic" title="Non-verbal magic" class="mw-redirect">non-verbal magic</a>, both of which required high amounts of mental strength. Moreover, in an alternate timeline, Snape was willing to sacrifice himself to defeat Voldemort and save the world once again, by distracting a swarm of <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a>, thereby giving <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a> the necessary opening to restore the timeline again.
</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Parents">Parents</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Lily Evans</b>: "<i>Doesn't your <a href="/wiki/Tobias_Snape" title="Tobias Snape">dad</a> like magic?</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>He doesn't like anything, much.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; Severus regarding his father's horrible personality<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div>
<p>Snape never regarded the place where he grew up as a home. Rather like <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> and Harry, <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> was his real home. It is likely that he suffered neglect as a child. His parents seem to have had a dysfunctional, even abusive relationship. This troubled, lonely childhood is strongly suggested to have accounted for his severe demeanour, depression, sadness, bitterness, and bouts of rage, as seen later in his life. 
</p><p>Despite having a father who disliked the wizarding community, Snape was quite skilled with magic before he even received his Hogwarts letter. Sirius Black would later remark that, when they first arrived at school, Snape knew more curses than many of the seventh-year students. It does seem that he had a slightly better relationship with his witch mother. During his school years, he nicknamed himself the "Half Blood Prince". In addition, it is quite likely <a href="/wiki/Eileen_Prince" title="Eileen Prince">Eileen</a> gave her son most, if not all of his school things. His <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_copy_of_Advanced_Potion-Making" title="Severus Snape's copy of Advanced Potion-Making">sixth-year Potions book</a> was, according to Harry, at least fifty years old. 
</p><p>Since at least 1996, Snape was staying in his family's home during the summers between school years. It is unknown what happened to his parents. As he was only thirty-six years old in 1996, his parents may well have been alive, but moved away and left the house to him. His salary as a Hogwarts professor probably made it possible for him to afford other lodging during summers, but his childhood memories of Lily may have stopped him from abandoning the house. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lily_Evans">Lily Evans</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Look...at....me....</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Snape wanting one last glimpse of Lily's eyes<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 161px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140712171247" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Lily Potter1"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Lily_Potter1.jpg" 	data-image-name="Lily Potter1.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/161?cb=20140712171247"  	 width="161"  	 height="220"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/161?cb=20140712171247" 	 alt="Lily Potter1"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Lily_Potter1.jpg" 	data-image-name="Lily Potter1.jpg" 	 	 width="161"  	 height="220"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lily_Potter1.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lily Evans, his once best friend and love of his life</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape's friendship with <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> was probably the only thing that truly brought joy to his life. He first met Lily at a very young age, recognising her as a witch one day as she and her sister <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Petunia</a> played in the park near his house; she had flown off the swings and made a flower grow from a sprout. Longing to escape his humiliating home life, Snape immediately sought to make her his friend. Despite the fact that Lily came from a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> family, he never truly saw her as being one of them because he was so smitten with her. 
</p><p>They spend time talking about magic and the wizarding world. Lily even asked if being Muggle-born matter in the Wizarding world, which Snape responded that it did not matter at all. In 1971, the two of them were accepted into <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> and continued a close friendship up until around their fifth year, despite being Sorted into different houses. Snape was very disappointed that they were not in the same house and forlorn because of it.
</p><p>During this time, Snape began hanging out with people who embraced Dark Magic and <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood_supremacy" title="Pure-blood supremacy">pure-blood supremacy</a>, which put a huge strain on their friendship. Lily was offended by many of the views that Snape was beginning to adopt and disliked the qualities that his new classmates were bringing out in him. Given time over again, Snape would never have done many of the things he did, but at the time he did not truly understand her aversion. He was so insecure and blinded by his attraction to the Dark side that he imagined she would find it impressive if he became a real Death Eater. Ironically, Lily might have grown to love Snape romantically (she certainly loved him as a friend) if he had not loved Dark Magic so much, and been drawn to such loathsome people and acts. When Snape called Lily a "<a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a>" in a moment of humiliation, it was the last straw for Lily. When she later asked him if he still intended to become a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> and he did not deny it, she severed all ties with him, despite Snape's profuse apologies.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/99/Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png/revision/latest?cb=20111026150555" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png" 	data-image-name="Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/99/Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111026150555"  	 width="250"  	 height="103"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/99/Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111026150555" 	 alt="Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png" 	data-image-name="Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png" 	 	 width="250"  	 height="103"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lily and Severus talking by the riverside</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Snape overheard <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney's first prophecy">the Prophecy</a>, he immediately relayed its contents to the <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Dark Lord</a>, not knowing that it would have anything to do with Lily. Upon discovering that Lord Voldemort was planning on targeting the Potter family, Snape pleaded with him to spare Lily in exchange for her husband and son. He later appealed to <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, asking him to do everything in his power to protect Lily and the rest of her family, if he had to.
</p><p>Snape was devastated by Lily's death, to the point of sinking into a depression that seemingly lasted the rest of his life. However, at Dumbledore's behest, he became committed to protecting her son Harry and assisting him in defeating the Dark Lord. Snape never spoke of Lily to anyone again, except for Dumbledore. This was likely due to heartbreak and worry that mention of her might make others suspicious. Even though he constantly slandered James to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Lily's son's</a> face, he alienated Lily from these attacks entirely, possibly due to his inability to ever insult her again. Indeed, Snape's Patronus was a doe, just like Lily's, because he loved her throughout his entire life. As Snape died, he asked Harry to look into his eyes; his last wish in his final moments was to die looking into the same green eyes that reminded him so much of Lily. 
</p><p>As a result of Snape's sacrifice of his own life, Lily's son Harry would name <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">her second grandson</a> after Snape. Coincidentally, said grandson would inherit Lily's green eyes. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Marauders">The Marauders</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)"><b>Snape</b>: "<i>You and Black, you're two of a kind, sentimental children forever whining about how bitterly unfair your lives have been. Well, it may have escaped your notice, but life </i>isn't<i> fair. Your blessed father knew that; in fact he frequently </i>saw<i> to it!</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>My father was a great man!</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>Your father was a </i>swine<i>!</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; Exchange between Harry and Snape during an <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">occlumency</a> <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_Severus_Snape%27s_private_lessons" title="Harry Potter and Severus Snape's private lessons">lesson</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 235px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Marauders_1997.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080414050923" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Marauders 1997"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Marauders_1997.jpg" 	data-image-name="Marauders 1997.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Marauders_1997.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20080414050923"  	 width="235"  	 height="186"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Marauders_1997.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20080414050923" 	 alt="Marauders 1997"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Marauders_1997.jpg" 	data-image-name="Marauders 1997.jpg" 	 	 width="235"  	 height="186"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Marauders_1997.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a>, his school bullies and enemies</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Marauders were a group of four <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> boys, with whom Severus began a relationship of enmity and hatred throughout their school years. The group consisted of <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>. Severus and the first two Marauders detested each other almost instantly upon meeting for the first time in a compartment on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>. Throughout their times at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, James and his friends (except for Lupin) bullied Snape ceaselessly, Pettigrew only did it though because James and Sirius did it. Lupin did not encourage the harassment, but he did not try to stop them, either. Snape, in turn, never lost an opportunity to get one up on them whenever possible. 
</p><p>However, James Potter ended up saving his life when Sirius told Snape how to get into the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a>. Snape caught a glimpse of Lupin transforming into a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> before James pulled him back through the tunnel. Snape did not think James was acting nobly. Rather, he saw it as being more of a self-serving act in order to avoid him and the rest of the Marauders being expelled from Hogwarts, and the incident only made him resent James more than ever. He also came to resent Lupin, believing that he had been in on Sirius's prank. 
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 235px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111027074415" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="MaraudersPickingOnSnape"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg" 	data-image-name="MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20111027074415"  	 width="235"  	 height="165"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20111027074415" 	 alt="MaraudersPickingOnSnape"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg" 	data-image-name="MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg" 	 	 width="235"  	 height="165"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Marauders bullying Snape during their time at Hogwarts</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Remus Lupin</b>: "<i>Well, Snape was a special case. I mean, he never lost an opportunity to curse James so you couldn't really expect James to take that lying down, could you?</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>And my mum was </i>OK<i> with that?</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Sirius Black</b>: "<i>She didn't know too much about it, to tell you the truth, I mean, James didn't take Snape on dates with her and jinx him in front of her, did he?</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; Lupin, Harry, and Sirius Black discussing Snape's interactions with Harry's parents during their seventh year<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div>
<p>During their seventh year at Hogwarts, Lily and James began dating, which probably fuelled Snape's hatred of him even more. James always suspected that Snape had deeper feelings for Lily, which factored strongly into his behaviour towards him. Snape's continued bitterness toward the Marauders, even into adulthood, became apparent in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, when Remus Lupin was given the position of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor at Hogwarts, despite Snape and Dumbledore both knowing that he was a werewolf.
</p><p>During the time that Harry Potter attended the school, Snape delighted in comparing Harry to his father and telling him that he was not the great man he liked to believe he was. Although Snape's descriptions of James' teenage self were accurate, Snape purposefully omitted even vague descriptions of the noble person James became. Snape mostly felt bitterness and resentment towards Remus Lupin and took to dropping hints about his being a werewolf in the hopes that the students would catch on. However, it should be noted that, despite Snape's strained relationship with the Marauders, he dutifully concocted potions for Remus Lupin during his tenure at Hogwarts and attempted to save his life during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Flight From Little Whinging</a>. Lupin was the only one of the Marauders who could interact with Snape at least on a perfunctory level when they were adults. Lupin, like everyone, believed Snape an evil, cowardly servant of Voldemort's after Snape killed Albus Dumbledore, and died before learning the truth. 
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 245px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Snape_Sirius.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111108153715" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Snape Sirius"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Snape_Sirius.jpg" 	data-image-name="Snape Sirius.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Snape_Sirius.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20111108153715"  	 width="245"  	 height="135"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Snape_Sirius.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20111108153715" 	 alt="Snape Sirius"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Snape_Sirius.jpg" 	data-image-name="Snape Sirius.jpg" 	 	 width="245"  	 height="135"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape_Sirius.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape confronts Sirius Black at the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape held an especially strong enmity towards Sirius. Although Snape's hatred towards Sirius for the humiliation he put him under alongside James in their Hogwarts years was already great, the fact that Sirius apparently was the Marauder who betrayed Lily to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> made him hate Sirius even more than he did with James. He was eager to be the one to hand Sirius over to receive the <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor's Kiss">Dementor's Kiss</a> after he <a href="/wiki/Azkaban_escapes#1993" title="Azkaban escapes">broke out</a> of <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> and was furious when he managed to escape yet again. After Sirius's innocence was proven, however, Dumbledore insisted that the two of them shake hands and ally together against Voldemort. Nevertheless, they remained barely capable of civilly conversing, as both of them still resented each other and Snape, in particular, taunted him about his uselessness to the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order</a> while confined to <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">his mother's house</a>, which escalated in Sirius nearly challenging Snape to a duel, which Snape was eager to and would have gladly accepted had the Weasleys not barged in. However, Sirius himself admitted he felt ashamed of his previous treatment and did not at all enjoy the reminder of the reason for Snape being humiliated due to Sirius being bored in their fifth year. Snape also, even if begrudgingly, accepted that they were fighting for the same side and was quick to check if Sirius was in fact safe after Harry reported to him he saw Sirius tortured by Voldemort and in the Ministry to be forced to retrieve the object.
</p><p>Although Snape's relationship with Pettigrew in their school years was already hostile, upon knowing he was the Marauder who truly betrayed Lily, he most likely became the Marauder Snape resented the most. Although forced to keep his dislike as best as he could due to his job as a double-agent for Dumbledore, Snape seized his chance to torment Pettigrew when the Dark Lord later assigned Pettigrew to work as his assistant, treating him like a slave, forcing him to clean his house and serve food to his guests, clearly intent on making sure that Pettigrew would not experience any comfortableness while under his command. Snape also seemed to enjoy threatening Pettigrew by telling Voldemort that he desired more dangerous assignments whenever he would protest his position as Snape's servant.
</p><p>In an ironic twist, despite their mutual antipathy, James' <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">second grandson</a> would be named after Snape years after the deaths of Snape and the Marauders.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Harry_Potter">Harry Potter</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>He is his father all over again.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Snape's assessment of Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 165px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140603201724" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Harry Potter"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Harry_Potter.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry Potter.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20140603201724"  	 width="165"  	 height="220"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20140603201724" 	 alt="Harry Potter"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Harry_Potter.jpg" 	data-image-name="Harry Potter.jpg" 	 	 width="165"  	 height="220"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, his former student and the person he sought to protect</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>From the day Harry set foot in Hogwarts, he and Snape loathed each other. Despite the fact that Snape was committed to honouring <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily</a>'s sacrifice, he could not bring himself to judge the boy objectively because of his connection to <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>, who bullied him in his school days. Indeed, Snape was filled with nothing but contempt and bitterness towards Harry, who simultaneously reminded him of both Lily and James. Harry served as living proof of the fact that Lily had given her <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a> to someone else, and Snape wasted no time in comparing him continually with his father.
</p><p>During Harry's time at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, Snape treated Harry viciously, both in class and out. He frequently derided the boy's abilities, bullied him in class, and punished him whenever possible. He was also resentful and even somewhat envious of Harry's popularity, which he also equated with Harry's father. Although Snape threatened to have Harry expelled more than once, he never attempted to follow through — presumably because it would have led to Harry losing the protection surrounding him. However, never did he forget that Harry was also Lily's child, and much beyond bureaucratic rules, this led him to put the boy's safety in the most critical situation. When he learned that <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> had intended for Harry to die all along, Severus remained horrified, seeing it as a calculated betrayal to Lily's memory.
</p><p>When Harry helped <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> escape, their relationship went under further strain, since Snape believed at that time that Sirius betrayed Lily to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> whereas Harry had learned of his innocence, although Snape continued to put Harry's safety first. During the brief period in which Snape gave private <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> lessons, Snape relished in forcing Harry to relive his worst memories. During the early years, Harry associated Snape with his abusive and bullying ways but when Sirius died, Harry took a savage pleasure in blaming Snape for having taunted Sirius about being useless, causing him to leave his hiding place and join the battle. 
</p><p>Though Snape came to the aid of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order</a> as swiftly as possible, Harry blamed Snape mainly to ease his own guilty conscience about the entire incident. However, this was nothing in comparison to the retroactive rage Harry felt upon finding out that Snape was the one who relayed <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney's first prophecy">the Prophecy</a> to Lord Voldemort, causing him to hunt down Harry and his family. When he later killed Dumbledore, the hatred between them was sealed almost as personally as between Harry and Voldemort.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 243px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122215347" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg" 	data-image-name="Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20141122215347"  	 width="243"  	 height="128"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20141122215347" 	 alt="Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg" 	data-image-name="Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg" 	 	 width="243"  	 height="128"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape looks into Harry's eyes as he dies</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As he lay dying, Snape told Harry to look at him and died looking into Lily's eyes. Following this, Harry was given access to all of Snape's concealed memories, which brought the former teacher's true intentions and more human side to light. When Harry discovered the love Snape had for his mother and the constant danger he put himself in to ensure his safety, his opinion of him changed completely.
</p><p>By adulthood, all of Harry's hatred of Snape seems to have vanished and it looks as though he had never harboured it at all. This can be seen through his request that a <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_portrait" title="Severus Snape's portrait">portrait of Snape</a> be hung in the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_office" title="Headmaster's office" class="mw-redirect">Headmaster's office</a> at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, which was not done immediately after Snape's death since he had abandoned his post. Furthermore, Harry gave his youngest son the name "Albus Severus", and told him that his Slytherin namesake was "<i>the bravest man I ever knew</i>."
