</p><p>Another aspect of Snape's highly visible, almost cartoonish mistreatment of Harry is that he knew all his actions might one day be reported to Voldemort by <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> spies. He did nothing that would create the image of real sympathy or loyalty to Potter or any of Voldemort's former adversaries, only curt professionalism towards his colleagues, obedience but not true loyalty to Dumbledore, and utter hatred for Harry. His need to behave this way was redoubled when it became clear Voldemort could use legilimency to read Harry's mind, and in doing so view any action by Snape in view of Harry. 
</p><p>Ironically, the two shared many similarities that neither of them was aware of. Both were <a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">half-blood</a> wizards who grew up among <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggles</a>. Both of their Muggle caretakers were cruel to them (Snape's father was implied to be abusive to Snape and his mother, while the <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">Dursleys</a> were neglectful towards Harry). Both Snape and Harry's childhoods involved <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Petunia Evans</a> (Snape was friends with Petunia's sister Lily, while Harry was Petunia's nephew and was raised (albeit reluctantly and abusively) by her). Both grew up wearing secondhand clothes (however, Snape was likely forced to wear them due to his family's poverty, while Harry's relatives simply refused to afford any major expenses on him). In addition, the two grew up virtually friendless until attending Hogwarts (Snape due to his unstable family life and secondhand clothes, Harry due to his relatives isolating him). 
</p><p>Upon entering Hogwarts, Snape and Harry were bullied mercilessly, in Snape's case, by the <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a> (who were led by James Potter), and Harry by (ironically) Snape himself, <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, among others. Furthermore, both had at least one near-death experience during their Hogwarts: Snape was nearly killed in an abortive prank by the <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a>, while Harry repeatedly had Voldemort attempting to kill him. However, both Snape and Harry had at least one silver gleaming: their genuinely intense and close romantic attraction to a redheaded teenager (Lily Evans and Ginny Weasley, respectively). Of course, while Snape did not marry Lily (who had married James and mothered Harry), Harry himself did marry Ginny (with whom he had a son named <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus</a>).
</p><p>In the second alternate timeline created by Scorpius Malfoy and Albus Potter, Scorpius revealed to Snape the predicament he had caused among other things. It is founded that Snape was extremely saddened and disappointed in his failure to protect Harry from Voldemort in the final battle, and was also engaged in assisting <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius</a> in fixing the timeline so Harry was alive and Voldemort defeated. One of the details he revealed after convincing Snape of his tale was that in his timeline that Harry had named his second son after him. This deeply touched Severus, who later told Scorpius to convey to Albus in the original timeline that he is proud that the boy carries his name and legacy, feeling apart of time he will never experience for the greater good of the world. He died without hesitation for the better world that Scorpius sought to restore, knowing his purpose could finally be served. Snape once again died for the legacy of his love, showing the kind of man he was at heart.
</p><p>After the original timeline was restored, Harry visited Cedric Diggory's grave with Albus, describing his son's two namesakes — Dumbledore and Snape — as very much alike, despite their sorting into different houses: <i>"great men, with huge flaws, and you know what - those flaws almost made them greater."</i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ron_Weasley_and_Hermione_Granger">Ron Weasley and Hermione Granger</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban"><b>Snape</b>: "<i>That is the second time you have spoken out of turn, Miss Granger... Five more points from Gryffindor for being an insufferable know-it-all.</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>You asked us a question and she knows the answer! Why ask if you don't want to be told?</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>Detention, Weasley... and if I ever hear you criticise the way I teach a class again, you will be very sorry indeed.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; A typical interaction in Snape's classroom<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 165px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191008170323" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" 	data-image-name="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20191008170323"  	 width="165"  	 height="222"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20191008170323" 	 alt="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" 	data-image-name="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" 	 	 width="165"  	 height="222"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron and Hermione in their first year</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape criticised <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> whenever possible, most likely because of the fact that they were friends of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> as well as being <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindors</a>. Although Snape seldom found anything wrong with Hermione's work and marked her grades accordingly, he never awarded her <a href="/wiki/House_points" title="House points">house points</a> and sometimes accused her of being an "<i>insufferable know-it-all</i>". Despite this, Snape saved their lives in 1993 when Professor Lupin had transformed into a werewolf at the full moon, and even after they had stopped being his students, continued to assist the three of them in their quest to destroy the seven Horcruxes (without them being any the wiser, of course). 
</p><p>It is unknown how Ron and Hermione reacted to the revelation of Snape's loyalty though as Harry recounted Snape's memories they were described as shocked. There's also no mention of them protesting Harry and Ginny naming their (Ron &amp; Hermione) nephew after Snape, which might indicate they came to forgive and admire him.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Albus_Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>I prefer not to put all my secrets in one basket, particularly not a basket that spends so much time dangling on the arm of Lord Voldemort.</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>Which I do on your orders!</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>And you do it extremely well. Do not think that I underestimate the constant danger in which you place yourself, Severus. To give Voldemort what appears to be valuable information while withholding the essentials is a job I would entrust to nobody but you.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; Dumbledore and Snape on the latter's espionage<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 165px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" 	data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220412"  	 width="165"  	 height="223"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220412" 	 alt="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" 	data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" 	 	 width="165"  	 height="223"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, his former headmaster</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape's relationship with Dumbledore was one of close, but not indefinite trust. Dumbledore was Snape's headmaster whilst at Hogwarts and was presumably impressed with Snape's academia and abilities. Snape likely felt no real loyalty to Dumbledore as a student and may have resented the latter's failure for stopping the torturous bullying Snape received at the hands of the Marauders. Despite this, he agreed to keep Remus Lupin's lycanthropy a secret when the headmaster ordered him (though likely out of self-serving reasons). Before allying himself with Snape, Dumbledore viewed him with, in his own words, disgust, for the latter's selfishness.
</p><p>After having accidentally put Lily's life in jeopardy by delivering a prophecy to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> (without knowing at the time that it was referring to her son), Snape turned to Dumbledore to keep her safe. Dumbledore chose to capitalise on Snape's remorse and initiated him into the Order of the Phoenix as a double agent. He also gave Snape the job of Potions Master and Head of Slytherin at Hogwarts at the tender age of 21.
</p><p>As a spy for the Order, Snape silently kept his place within the ranks of the Death Eaters, while informing Dumbledore about their movements. He also adopted the role of secret agent for Voldemort and supplied him with strategic scraps of information about the Order. The content of these reports was often dictated by Dumbledore. It is implied that Snape withheld little if any, information from Dumbledore that was relevant to the Order's success, while Snape deliberately did the opposite for Voldemort.
</p><p>Snape resented Dumbledore's secrecy and was offended by this perceived lack of faith in his abilities. However, when Snape discovered that Dumbledore had intended for Harry to die all along, he was horrified, seeing it as a calculated betrayal of Lily's memory. Dumbledore clearly underestimated the depth of Snape's feelings, and, years later, was very surprised to learn that he still maintained his devotion.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 160px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160819104925" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Snape and Dumbledore"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg" 	data-image-name="Snape and Dumbledore.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20160819104925"  	 width="160"  	 height="240"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20160819104925" 	 alt="Snape and Dumbledore"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg" 	data-image-name="Snape and Dumbledore.jpg" 	 	 width="160"  	 height="240"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">"<i>I am fortunate, extremely fortunate, that I have you, Severus...</i>"</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Dumbledore became aware of Voldemort's plan to kill him. Knowing Voldemort expected <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> to fail, and assuming Snape to be Draco's successor, Dumbledore assigned Snape the task of killing him when the situation arose. Snape was genuinely reluctant to do this and even stated when Dumbledore stated that it was necessary to protect Draco's soul that his soul may very well be damaged from such an act, showing Snape had grew to genuinely care for the Headmaster. Even with the revelation of Dumbledore's true plans for Harry, Snape hesitated for a time before carrying out his mission, his face being described as holding disgust and hatred for himself for what he was about to do. Dumbledore also entrusted Snape with protecting the students once Hogwarts fell into Voldemort's control.
</p><p>In spite of their mutual trust in each other, Dumbledore never allowed Snape his coveted position as Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher. It was claimed that he did it so that Snape wouldn't experience a resurgence of "old habits". The truth may in fact be that Dumbledore believed the post to be <a href="/wiki/Jinx" title="Jinx">jinxed</a> by Lord Voldemort after <i>he</i> failed to attain the post, and this jinx had prevented any teacher from lasting beyond a year. To place Snape in such a position might have risked his safety, and Dumbledore would not have permitted such a risk, in case he required Snape's aid against Voldemort again. When Dumbledore was infected by the curse on Marvolo Gaunt's ring, he asked Snape to kill him. Knowing that such an act would vilify Snape beyond any doubt in the mind of the Wizarding public, Dumbledore allowed Snape the position because he would have to leave immediately anyway.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Petunia_Evans">Petunia Evans</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>You and that Snape boy ... weirdos, that's what you two are!</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Petunia Evans insulting <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">her sister</a> and Snape<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 160px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Petunia_Dursley_POA.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160721182515" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Petunia Dursley POA"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Petunia_Dursley_POA.jpg" 	data-image-name="Petunia Dursley POA.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Petunia_Dursley_POA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20160721182515"  	 width="160"  	 height="216"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Petunia_Dursley_POA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20160721182515" 	 alt="Petunia Dursley POA"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Petunia_Dursley_POA.jpg" 	data-image-name="Petunia Dursley POA.jpg" 	 	 width="160"  	 height="216"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Petunia_Dursley_POA.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Petunia Evans</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape first met <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Petunia Evans</a> during their childhood. She was the sister of <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a>, but Petunia was a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a>, unlike her sister. Snape and Petunia strongly disliked each other, from the first moment they met. Petunia, who was contemptuous of anything out of the ordinary, viewed him with disdain because of his poor economic status and because he was such an oddball. Snape, on the other hand, regarded her balefully because she was a Muggle, and because she made disparaging comments about his clothes. It is unknown how Petunia reacted to (or if she even ever knew about) Snape calling Lily a <a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a>, but it can assumed that this incident caused Petunia to hate him even more.
</p><p>Ironically, Petunia and Snape's negative encounters with each other as children and adolescents helped lay the foundations for their respective adult personalities. It is possible that Petunia's interactions with Snape exacerbated her already growing disdain for the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">Wizarding world</a> and eventual estrangement with Lily. Likewise, Snape's antipathy towards Petunia helped fuel his dislike towards Muggles in general, causing him to experiment with <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood_supremacy" title="Pure-blood supremacy">Pure-blood supremacy</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a>, culminating in his recruitment in the Death Eaters. Even more tragically, Snape's actions as a Death Eater caused the death of Petunia's sister Lily to be murdered by Voldemort, which in turn caused Petunia to grudgingly adopt (and abuse and neglect) her nephew <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>. 
</p><p>Years after Snape's death, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">one</a> of Petunia's great-nephews would be named after Snape. It is unknown if she had known about this, given how she likely severed contact with Harry after he left her house. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lord_Voldemort">Lord Voldemort</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Severus Snape wasn't yours. Snape was Dumbledore's. Dumbledore's from the moment you starting hunting down my mother. And you never realised it, because of the thing you can't understand ... he loved her for nearly all of his life. </i>"
</dd><dd><b>Lord Voldemort</b>: "<i>It matters not! It matters not whether Snape was mine or Dumbledore's, or what petty obstacles they tried to put in my path! I crushed them as I crushed your mother, Snape's supposed great love!</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> regarding Snape's duplicity<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 156px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Voldemort1998.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220615" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Voldemort1998"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Voldemort1998.jpg" 	data-image-name="Voldemort1998.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Voldemort1998.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20141122220615"  	 width="156"  	 height="238"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Voldemort1998.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20141122220615" 	 alt="Voldemort1998"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Voldemort1998.jpg" 	data-image-name="Voldemort1998.jpg" 	 	 width="156"  	 height="238"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort1998.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lord Voldemort, his former master and eventual killer</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In his days as a Death Eater, Snape was one of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s most trusted and devoted servants. In 1980, Snape overheard part of a <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney's first prophecy">prophecy</a> foretelling Voldemort's downfall. After being caught, Snape hurried to tell Voldemort what he had heard, unaware that his information was incomplete. However, he turned against the Dark Lord the moment he decided to target <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a>.
</p><p>When Voldemort returned to physical form in 1995, Snape ostensibly returned to him as a spy for the Order. Using <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a>, Snape was able to close his mind, hide his true allegiance and maintain his cover as a faithful Death Eater. Snape was one of the only Death Eaters to have the Dark Lord's complete trust and, after he <a href="/wiki/Funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore#Dumbledore.27s_death" title="Funeral of Albus Dumbledore">murdered</a> Albus Dumbledore, he became Voldemort's most trusted adviser. He was held in such high regard that Voldemort accepted making him Headmaster of Hogwarts after seizing power.
</p><p>However, Voldemort coldly had <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">his snake</a>, Nagini, kill Snape in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, believing it would make him the true master of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a>. Although he claimed he regretted its necessity, he felt no remorse over murdering one of his most faithful advisors. After Snape's death, Harry Potter revealed to Voldemort that Snape had managed to deceive him for years because he acted entirely out of love for <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> — something Voldemort neither understood or cared about. Indeed, at the time Snape asked Voldemort to spare Lily's life, he erroneously believed that Snape's interest in her was merely physical, and callously stated that there were other women "of purer blood, worthier of him" after her death. Voldemort also reacted with indifference to Snape's true loyalties, as Voldemort mistakenly believed that Snape's death made Voldemort the master of the Elder Wand. This error soon cost Voldemort his own life while ensuring that Snape's sacrifice was not in vain.
</p><p>It is possible that part of the reason Voldemort put so much trust in Snape was because he identified with his background. Both were the only children of Muggle fathers and <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a> mothers (Voldemort: <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle_Senior" title="Tom Riddle Senior">Tom Riddle Snr</a> and <a href="/wiki/Merope_Riddle" title="Merope Riddle">Merope Gaunt</a>; Snape: <a href="/wiki/Tobias_Snape" title="Tobias Snape">Tobias Snape</a> and <a href="/wiki/Eileen_Prince" title="Eileen Prince">Eileen Prince</a>). Both Muggle men had nothing but hatred for their sons and wives and neglected their sons and as a consequence both Riddle and Snape yearned to shed their unhappy beginnings. Voldemort's father had abandoned his wife when she was pregnant with their son, while Snape's father was abusive towards his wife and their young son. Both Riddle and Snape claimed greater identification with their maternal lineage than their paternal ancestry —the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Gaunt" title="House of Gaunt">Gaunt family</a> and <a href="/wiki/Prince_family" title="Prince family">Prince family</a>, respectively. Both men grew up in poverty — Voldemort grew up in an <a href="/wiki/Wool%27s_Orphanage" title="Wool's Orphanage">orphanage</a>, while Snape lived in <a href="/wiki/Spinner%27s_End" title="Spinner's End">Spinner's End</a>.
</p><p>In addition, both Riddle and Snape were Sorted into <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a>, and were known for their intelligence. Both men had a passion for the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a> and <a href="/wiki/Blood_status" title="Blood status">blood purity</a> as childhood, and bestowed grandiose titles onto themselves (Riddle was known as Lord Voldemort, while Snape adopted the name the Half-Blood Prince). Both saw <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> as sort of a real home as opposed to their default home. In addition, both men kept a book related to the Dark Arts in their sixteenth years — Voldemort had the <a href="/wiki/T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary" title="T. M. Riddle's Diary">diary</a> that he converted into a <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>, while Snape had a <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_copy_of_Advanced_Potion-Making" title="Severus Snape's copy of Advanced Potion-Making">Potions textbook</a> that he used to write original magic. Lastly both were part of a <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_gang" title="Tom Riddle's gang">gang of fu</a><a href="/wiki/Gang_of_Slytherins" title="Gang of Slytherins">ture Death Eaters</a> who bullied their fellow students. Voldemort may have seen him as a trusted Death Eater who shared the same hatred for his father as he had for his own. The only major thing that differs between Voldemort and Snape's relationships with their fathers is murder; Voldemort had murdered his own father while Snape did <i>not</i> murder his. Voldemort must have also recognised Snape as a powerful and intelligent wizard, traits which would manifest as usefulness to his ideology.
</p><p>However, there were other differences between Snape and Voldemort. Snape had a secret love for <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> for most of his life, which motivated him to defect from the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> and protect her <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">son</a> after her <a href="/wiki/Attack_at_Godric%27s_Hollow_(1981)" title="Attack at Godric's Hollow (1981)">death</a> at Voldemort's hands. Voldemort, on the other hand, disregarded love as a weakness that was beyond his comprehension, and had allegiance to only himself. This had coincidentally led to his own undoing. In addition, unlike Voldemort, Snape had known about the existence of the wizarding world before he was eleven years old (likely due to the fact that Snape's mother was actually present in his childhood).
</p><p>Snape possessed the ability of independent flight, which was presumably taught to him by Lord Voldemort as he displayed the same ability during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>. This shows that Lord Voldemort had a great deal of trust in Snape as he taught him a very unique ability, something he might not have done with any other <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weasley_family">Weasley family</span></h3>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 236px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/806px-Weasley-family.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120731222117" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="806px-Weasley-family"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="806px-Weasley-family.jpg" 	data-image-name="806px-Weasley-family.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/806px-Weasley-family.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20120731222117"  	 width="236"  	 height="164"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/806px-Weasley-family.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20120731222117" 	 alt="806px-Weasley-family"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="806px-Weasley-family.jpg" 	data-image-name="806px-Weasley-family.jpg" 	 	 width="236"  	 height="164"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:806px-Weasley-family.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Weasley family</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Weasleys had a neutral if not unkind relationship with Snape. The Weasleys were blood-traitors, supporters of Muggles and Muggle-borns and opposed to the Dark Arts, all things Snape held opposite views towards as a Death Eater. Snape had relinquished most prejudices after switching sides though. It is unknown if Snape was still loyal to the Death Eaters when <a href="/wiki/Fabian_Prewett" title="Fabian Prewett">Fabian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gideon_Prewett" title="Gideon Prewett">Gideon Prewett</a> were killed or if he had defected before their deaths. Both events occurred in <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>. The Weasleys, like Snape in his youth, were profusely financially strained. Molly and Arthur had left Hogwarts before Snape started but knew him through their membership in the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order</a>. They seemed to, like most, trust him because Dumbledore did. Little is known about their relationship, although Molly, at least, did not let Snape's maltreatment of her children staunch her respect for him as a teacher. Given Molly was a good potioneer, this could have helped her find some common ground with him.  
</p><p>Snape taught seven Weasleys at Hogwarts. <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a> and <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy</a>, despite being Gryffindors, earned many <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.s</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.s</a>, showing Snape did not forsake his professionalism for his bias. Despite this, Ginny mentioned once that Bill and Snape did not get along when Bill was a student. There was, in fact, only a decade separating Snape and Bill. Fred and George irked Snape profusely with their pranks and disinterest in school work. Interestingly, they were their generation's <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a>, map and all, and as such Snape may have viewed them as a reincarnation of his childhood bullies. It is mentioned the twins got many detentions and house point losses which were likely Snape's doing.
</p><p>Ginny was the final Weasley to attend Hogwarts before Snape's death and she bared a remarkable resemblance to Lily. She was also the only remaining Weasley at Hogwarts during Snape's time as headmaster and co-lead the reformed Dumbledore's Army, unknowingly allying herself with Snape. Notably Snape seemed as worried as the other teachers when Ginny was taken into the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>.
</p><p>Ron knew of Snape's treatment of students before attending his classes, likely hearing it from an older sibling indicating a long string of antagonism between Snape and the Weasley children. Snape's murder of Dumbledore in close conjunction of Bill being maimed by <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Greyback</a> and accidently maiming George gave birth to the families hatred of him. However, when the war was over, the Weasley's learned of Snape's true loyalties and likely grew to respect &amp; admire him. A new <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">member</a> of the family was eventually named for him.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Malfoy_family">Malfoy family</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Lucius always spoke highly of you.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> during Snape's class inspection<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 165px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Malfoys.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080512050348" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Malfoys"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Malfoys.jpg" 	data-image-name="Malfoys.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Malfoys.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20080512050348"  	 width="165"  	 height="230"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Malfoys.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20080512050348" 	 alt="Malfoys"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Malfoys.jpg" 	data-image-name="Malfoys.jpg" 	 	 width="165"  	 height="230"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Malfoys.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius</a> and <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, whom he was on good terms with</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape appeared to be on good terms with the <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">Malfoy family</a>. Lucius Malfoy was a <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a> when Snape began attending Hogwarts, and the two ran in the same social circles, which included other future <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. Snape and Lucius likely worked together as Death Eaters during the First Wizarding War. It's unknown if Lucius was suspicious of Snape's true allegiance, though he most likely believed Snape to be truly loyal to Voldemort. Lucius continued to think and speak well of Snape later in life. Perhaps because of this, Snape also favoured Lucius's son Draco. Draco seemed to look up to Snape, once sycophantically saying that he would make a far better Headmaster than <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>.
</p><p>However, after his father's imprisonment in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> following the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, Draco came to resent and mistrust Snape, suspecting that he was trying to usurp his father's place in the Death Eater ranks. He refused Snape's repeated offers of help with <a href="/wiki/Plot_to_assassinate_Albus_Dumbledore" title="Plot to assassinate Albus Dumbledore">the task</a> <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> assigned him in his sixth year. <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa Malfoy</a>, on the other hand, begged Snape to assist Draco in his task to assassinate Dumbledore, fearing that her son was being set up to fail. She ignored the warnings of her sister, <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, who did not trust Snape, and had him make an <a href="/wiki/Unbreakable_Vow" title="Unbreakable Vow">Unbreakable Vow</a> to help Draco and take over the task should he fail. This speaks highly as to the trust and respect the Malfoys had for Snape.
</p><p>It's unknown how the Malfoys reacted upon learning of Snape's death and true loyalties. They were possibly saddened due to their longtime friendship. It's possible that they were also sympathetic due to their own disillusionment from Voldemort.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bellatrix_Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>I don't trust you, Snape, as you very well know!</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Bellatrix Lestrange's distrust of Snape<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 164px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140622235902" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Bellatrix Lestrange promo"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg" 	data-image-name="Bellatrix Lestrange promo.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/164?cb=20140622235902"  	 width="164"  	 height="229"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/164?cb=20140622235902" 	 alt="Bellatrix Lestrange promo"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg" 	data-image-name="Bellatrix Lestrange promo.jpg" 	 	 width="164"  	 height="229"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, whom he had little patience for</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Unlike her Malfoy relatives, Bellatrix Lestrange invested none of her faith in Snape. It's possible that the two got along better during the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a> as Sirius once described the two as old acquaintances; however, later in life, she showed nothing but distrust toward him. She saw right through his triple agent charade, even though <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> could not. Part of the reason for this may have been Snape's <a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">half-blood</a> status and his avoidance of imprisonment in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>, while she was incarcerated there for years. Given Bellatrix's obsessive, slavish love for Voldemort, she may have envied the trust the Dark Lord put in Snape, whom she considered her inferior in both blood and service. 
</p><p>She was suspicious when Snape did not immediately return to Voldemort after his rebirth, and why he never took an opportunity to kill <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> when, as one of the boy's <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">professors</a>, he had easy access to him. When Snape easily backhanded all of her accusations, bringing up that Lord Voldemort himself interrogated him of those lines, Bellatrix was lost for words; Snape was cunning enough to use the power of mere words to render Bella such, for he knew that to further her doubt of Severus would, by extension, mean that she would also be doubting the Dark Lord. And she was too fanatical to let such disparity in opinion between herself and her master go too far. With her logical reasons for distrusting Snape were gone, her irrational jealousy was all she had left to give her a reason to hate him. For that reason it perhaps grew stronger. Bellatrix was uneasy speaking openly about things around Snape, and tried to discourage her <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">younger sister</a> from asking him for help with Draco's task. Although Bellatrix did not fear or respect Snape like most others did, she seemed to only avoid his bad side so as to avoid Voldemort's bad side by extention.
</p><p>Snape, on the other hand, seemed to regard Bellatrix coldly. He had very little patience for her dramatics and tendency towards hysteria. He even took the opportunity to mock her for her struggle against the six teenagers from <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore's Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, and that she was losing her status in Voldemort's eyes. Snape and Bellatrix were Voldemort's most powerful and trusted servants (or so Voldemort thought as far as Snape was concerned) and as such they never picked a real fight with one another. They were also the Death Eaters that the Order of the Phoenix and its associates hated the most and the ones the other Death Eaters feared and respected the most. Bellatrix never managed to convince anyone of Snape's true loyalty and died moments before it was revealed to everyone that she had been right all along. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Igor_Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire"><b>Snape</b>: "<i>...don't see what there is to fuss about, Igor.</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Igor Karkaroff</b>: "<i>Severus, you cannot pretend this isn't happening! It's been getting clearer and clearer for months, I am becoming seriously concerned, I can't deny it—</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>Then flee. Flee, I will make your excuses. I, however, am remaining at Hogwarts.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; Snape and Karkaroff speaking in private during the Yule Ball<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 160px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100724115703" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Igor Karkaroff GoF"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg" 	data-image-name="Igor Karkaroff GoF.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20100724115703"  	 width="160"  	 height="242"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20100724115703" 	 alt="Igor Karkaroff GoF"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg" 	data-image-name="Igor Karkaroff GoF.jpg" 	 	 width="160"  	 height="242"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape and Karkaroff had a little bit of history with each other from the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>. Karkaroff was captured by <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a> and during his trial, in a desperate attempt to avoid going to prison he gave to the Ministry many names of Death Eaters, including Snape. However, at the time he was not aware that Snape was a double agent. He desperately tried to convince the court that Snape remained guilty despite the judge telling him Snape was cleared.
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>, when Karkaroff's and Snape's Dark Marks were burning stronger, Karkaroff told his worries to Snape, who expressed little concern to him. As the year progressed, Karkaroff continued to pursue Snape over the issue, to which Snape became increasingly annoyed, and even started to evade him. Snape described Karkaroff as cowardly and had no intention of joining him in hiding once Voldemort returned. Karkaroff's death did not seem to surprise Snape.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Death_Eaters">Death Eaters</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>...you and your precious little Death Eater friends — you see, you don’t even deny it! You don’t even deny that’s what you’re all aiming to be! You can’t wait to join You-Know-Who, can you?</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Lily Evans on the day she and Snape had their falling out<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 166px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091129164509" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Unidentified Death Eater (II)"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg" 	data-image-name="Unidentified Death Eater (II).jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20091129164509"  	 width="166"  	 height="227"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20091129164509" 	 alt="Unidentified Death Eater (II)"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg" 	data-image-name="Unidentified Death Eater (II).jpg" 	 	 width="166"  	 height="227"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Unidentified_Death_Eater_(II).jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A masked <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Severus became a member of the Death Eaters after <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. During his time at school, he was member of a "gang of <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherins</a> that would later become Death Eaters". This gang included <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Black</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rodolphus_Lestrange" title="Rodolphus Lestrange">Rodolphus Lestrange</a>, <a href="/wiki/Avery_(Marauder-era)" title="Avery (Marauder-era)" class="mw-redirect">Avery</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mulciber_(Marauder-era)" title="Mulciber (Marauder-era)" class="mw-redirect">Mulciber</a>, <a href="/wiki/Evan_Rosier" title="Evan Rosier">Evan Rosier</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wilkes" title="Wilkes">Wilkes</a>. <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> could not understand how he could be friends with them, as they had an "evil sense of humour". It's unknown how close he really was with the members of this gang, however he did seem somewhat defensive when Lily spoke ill of Mulciber and Avery implying a possible level of intimacy with them at least. Rosier and Wilkes were killed by Aurors after the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>; Rodolphus, Bellatrix, and Mulciber were captured (but later escaped), while Avery managed to defect. Besides Bellatrix, it's unknown what kind of relationship he had with his old school friends as an adult.
</p><p>Other Death Eaters Snape knew were <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto Carrow</a>, two siblings. Judging by Amycus's reaction upon seeing Snape at the Astronomy Tower it seems that he (and possibly Alecto) truly believed that Snape was on their side. Amycus and Alecto were Deputy Headmasters at Hogwarts, at the time Snape was Headmaster. They were both sadistic, and they liked to torture the students who opposed them. They also ordered the students to practise the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> on punished students. Death Eater <a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Corban Yaxley</a> appeared to be friendly with Snape too however he seemed resentful when Voldemort valued Snape's information and accomplishments over his own. Along with <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>, they seemed to fear Snape's abilities, as they instantly stood down when he approached to kill Dumbledore, despite Draco being tasked with the job.
</p><p>Furthermore, Snape knew the extremely loyal Death Eater <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>. during the First Wizarding War. For many years, it was believed that Barty Crouch was dead. However, he escaped from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> and planned to send Harry Potter to Voldemort, who would be reborn. Snape, along with Dumbledore and McGonagall, saved Harry from Crouch while he was trying to kill Harry. Snape was surprised that Crouch was still alive. Later, the Death Eater was given the Dementor's Kiss though no reaction from Snape is noted.
</p><p>Other known Death Eaters were <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a>, <a href="/wiki/Augustus_Rookwood" title="Augustus Rookwood">Augustus Rookwood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nott" title="Nott">Nott</a>, <a href="/wiki/Crabbe" title="Crabbe">Crabbe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Goyle" title="Goyle">Goyle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Walden_Macnair" title="Walden Macnair">Walden Macnair</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jugson" title="Jugson">Jugson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thorfinn_Rowle" title="Thorfinn Rowle">Thorfinn Rowle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gibbon" title="Gibbon">Gibbon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rosier" title="Rosier">Rosier</a>, <a href="/wiki/Avery_(Riddle-era)" title="Avery (Riddle-era)" class="mw-redirect">Avery</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mulciber_(Riddle-era)" title="Mulciber (Riddle-era)" class="mw-redirect">Mulciber</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lestrange" title="Lestrange">Lestrange</a>, <a href="/wiki/Travers" title="Travers">Travers</a>, <a href="/wiki/Selwyn" title="Selwyn">Selwyn</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Rabastan_Lestrange" title="Rabastan Lestrange">Rabastan Lestrange</a>. Rodolphus and Rabastan were the only ones who tried to search for Lord Voldemort after the first defeat, along with Bellatrix and Barty Crouch Jnr During the Second Wizarding War. All those Death Eaters were either killed or imprisoned after Voldemort's final defeat. Although not shown interacting much with Snape, they all presumably held him in the same respect and fear that Yaxley &amp; Greyback did and, considering Snape's rank, had to answer to him. According to Snape some of them believed that he was not truly loyal to their cause, however none of them (save Bellatrix) openly confronted him about it.
</p><p>It is unknown how the surviving Death Eaters reacted — either as a group or as individuals — to reveal of Snape's demise (if they found out) or the revelations of his true <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">loyalties</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Neville_Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>Possibly no one's warned you, Lupin, but this class contains Neville Longbottom. I would advise you not to entrust him with anything difficult. Not unless Miss Granger is hissing instructions in his ear.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Severus Snape insults Neville in front of the other teachers<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 156px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140610141612" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Neville Longbottom"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Neville_Longbottom.jpg" 	data-image-name="Neville Longbottom.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20140610141612"  	 width="156"  	 height="243"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20140610141612" 	 alt="Neville Longbottom"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Neville_Longbottom.jpg" 	data-image-name="Neville Longbottom.jpg" 	 	 width="156"  	 height="243"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_Longbottom.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, his student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville Longbottom was perhaps one of the worst <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> students Snape ever taught. As such, Snape was especially cruel to him and often made a point of ridiculing his failures in class. On one occasion, Snape threatened to test Neville's <a href="/wiki/Shrinking_Solution" title="Shrinking Solution">Shrinking Solution</a> on his <a href="/wiki/Trevor" title="Trevor">pet toad</a>, despite the fact that the <a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">potion</a> would be poisonous if not brewed correctly. Even outside of his own classroom, Snape did not hesitate from offering harsh opinions of Neville.
</p><p>This treatment made Neville extremely nervous to be around Snape, and further contributed to his poor performance in <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a>. Neville admitted in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a> that Snape was his greatest fear, and, predictably, Snape was the form Neville's <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a> took at that time.
</p><p>Soon Snape heard about Neville's boggart and treated him, if possible, even worse than he usually did. However, in 1996, Snape alerted members of the Order of the Phoenix, in order to save Neville, Harry and their friends from Death Eaters. Although Snape helped save Neville's life, he continued to treat him poorly in school. Neville was surprised that Snape killed Dumbledore but did learn the truth later. Snape chose to do a subtle favour for Neville when he was caught along with Ginny Weasley and Luna Lovegood attempting to steal the Sword of Gryffindor. Snape chose to send Neville, Luna and Ginny to detention with their friend Hagrid rather than subject them to the sadistic forms of discipline practised by the Carrows. When Neville killed Nagini, he inadvertently avenged Snape's murder.
</p><p>Though it is possible that from <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a>'s first prophecy that it was either Neville or Harry who was to threaten Voldemort, that as a result with Voldemort going for the Potters, that Neville represented his guilt from revealing the prophecy to Voldemort and the potential alternative for what could've happened. As a result. from Snape's point of view, Neville embodied all of this and that made him detest and bully him.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Minerva_McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">"<i>Coward!</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;McGonagall attempts to apprehend Snape after he flees the castle during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 159px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150810172040" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Mcgonagall"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Mcgonagall.jpg" 	data-image-name="Mcgonagall.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/159?cb=20150810172040"  	 width="159"  	 height="226"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/159?cb=20150810172040" 	 alt="Mcgonagall"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Mcgonagall.jpg" 	data-image-name="Mcgonagall.jpg" 	 	 width="159"  	 height="226"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mcgonagall.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, his colleague and former professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva McGonagall was generally on good professional terms with Snape. However, seeing as Snape was the <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Slytherin_House" title="Head of Slytherin House">Head of Slytherin House</a>, while McGonagall was the <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Gryffindor_House" title="Head of Gryffindor House">Head of Gryffindor House</a>, there was some antagonism between them, as Snape usually teased McGonagall when Slytherin had more points than Gryffindor. McGonagall was also wary of the fact that Snape was once a Death Eater. However, she trusted him because she knew that Dumbledore trusted him, too. She also did not hesitate to call him out when she believed he was being too cruel. McGonagall, like Snape, was very strict, but much more fair, as noted by <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>. McGonagall was Snape's Transfiguration professor when he was a student and likely admired his brilliance.
</p><p>Her trust of Snape evaporated after <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a>'s murder. Furthermore, when Snape became Headmaster of Hogwarts, McGonagall tried to oppose him and the Carrows, without knowing that Snape was trying to protect the students from the Carrows, too. When the war was coming to a head, she personally attacked Snape and violently called him a coward, a trait she, as Head Of Gryffindor, loathed. It is unknown how she reacted when she learned about his true loyalties, but it is likely that she forgave him. She permitted <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_portrait" title="Severus Snape's portrait">his portrait</a> to be hung in the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_office" title="Headmaster's office" class="mw-redirect">Headmaster's office</a>, at Harry's request.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_staff">Hogwarts staff</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>Snape... we all wondered... but he trusted... always... </i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Professor McGonagall after Dumbledore's death<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 150px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/20100111183429%21Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png/revision/latest?cb=20100310181520" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="20100111183429!Flitwick HBPoster Lighter"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="20100111183429%21Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png" 	data-image-name="20100111183429!Flitwick HBPoster Lighter.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/20100111183429%21Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20100310181520"  	 width="150"  	 height="257"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/20100111183429%21Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20100310181520" 	 alt="20100111183429!Flitwick HBPoster Lighter"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="20100111183429%21Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png" 	data-image-name="20100111183429!Flitwick HBPoster Lighter.png" 	 	 width="150"  	 height="257"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:20100111183429!Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a>, his colleague and former professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape was respected professionally among his colleagues at Hogwarts. Though many of them exhibited some wariness towards him due to his status as a former Death Eater, they opted to trust him because Dumbledore did. When Snape killed Dumbledore, however, the entire staff was shocked. In 1998, Flitwick and Sprout, like many other teachers, tried to oppose Snape and the Carrows, and they were among the ones who chased Snape out of Hogwarts before the battle. Flitwick and Sprout were Snape's Charms and Herbology teachers respectively in the latter's youth.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> was no friend of Snape's but trusted him, mainly because Dumbledore trusted him and would always defend him whenever Harry or Ron would express their distrust for him. Both Hagrid and Snape became members of the first and second <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> and they both fought against Voldemort. When Snape killed Dumbledore, Hagrid initially disbelieved the fact and told Harry he must be mistaken but was later furious to learn that Snape had indeed killed the late Headmaster. Hagrid openly opposed Snape when he became the Headmaster of Hogwarts by holding a <a href="/wiki/Support_Harry_Potter_party" title="Support Harry Potter party">Support Harry Potter party</a> (unaware Snape was secretly still on their side), an act which almost resulted in his arrest and forced him to go into hiding until the final battle. Before Hagrid fled, Snape put students in detentions with Hagrid, ensuring that they were protected from the harsher and torturous punishments from the Carrows. However, Hagrid eventually learned of Snape's true loyalties during the final confrontation of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 160px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/Horace_Slughorn.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20121226172917" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Horace Slughorn"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Horace_Slughorn.jpg" 	data-image-name="Horace Slughorn.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/Horace_Slughorn.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20121226172917"  	 width="160"  	 height="251"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/Horace_Slughorn.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20121226172917" 	 alt="Horace Slughorn"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Horace_Slughorn.jpg" 	data-image-name="Horace Slughorn.jpg" 	 	 width="160"  	 height="251"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Horace_Slughorn.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, Severus's Head of House and Potions Professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape disliked most of the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> instructors, such as <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>, <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>. Though this was at least partially out of his own desire to teach the subject, he had legitimate reasons to dislike them, as Quirrell was an agent of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, Lockhart was a narcissistic fraud, Lupin had acted as a bystander to, if not directly participating in, much of the bullying Snape faced in his school days, and Umbridge was a corrupt woman who wanted the entire school under her thumb. The only <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor Snape refrained from displaying disrespect to was <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Bartemius Crouch Jnr</a> impersonating <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, the toughest <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark Wizard</a> hunter the Ministry ever had. Harry surmised this was out of fear, but it was more likely due to allegiance. It should be noted that Moody had been the one to kill <a href="/wiki/Evan_Rosier" title="Evan Rosier">Evan Rosier</a>, an old friend of Snape's, and possibly others. 
</p><p>Horace Slughorn had been Snape's Potions master and head of house. Snape was made a member of the Slug Club as he was a brilliant student and even then his potion abilities were almost as good if not equal to Slughorn's. Snape might have been the student to whom Slughorn once award a vial of Liquid Luck. It is highly unlikely that Slughorn was aware of Snape's self-altered textbook and was flabbergasted when Snape murdered Dumbledore.  
</p><p>Snape seemed on good terms with <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a>, the caretaker, who respected Snape, and like him, disliked most students at Hogwarts. Snape often had Filch report directly to him if he found anything suspicious during his nighttime patrols. It's possible that after Voldemort took over Filch was only able to remain at Hogwarts because of his loyalty towards Snape. It is unknown how Filch reacted when he learned that Snape killed <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a>, or when Snape himself died.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_students">Hogwarts students</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>You are here to learn the subtle science and exact art of potion-making. As there is little foolish wand-waving here, many of you will hardly believe this is magic. I don't expect you will really understand the beauty of the softly simmering cauldron with its shimmering fumes, the delicate power of liquids that creep through human veins, bewitching the mind, ensnaring the senses... I can teach you how to bottle fame, brew glory, even put a stopper in death — if you aren't as big a bunch of dunderheads as I usually have to teach.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;Snape talking to the students at his first lesson<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone">[src]</a></sup>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 240px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123060553" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Dumbledore&amp;#039;s Army"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg" 	data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20161123060553"  	 width="240"  	 height="160"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20161123060553" 	 alt="Dumbledore&amp;#039;s Army"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg" 	data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" 	 	 width="240"  	 height="160"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Some of Snape's students</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape was not popular among the majority of the students at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. He was quite strict and had high standards. He refused to allow any students into his <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.</a>-level Potions classes unless they achieved an "O" grade on their O.W.L. exam for the subject (many other Hogwarts teachers would still accept the next-best grade, "E", for their advanced classes). Despite N.E.W.T.s not beginning until the sixth-year, it was Snape's policy to grade his fifth-year students by the N.E.W.T. scale. At the beginning of the 1995-1996 school year, he warned his fifth-year students that he expected everyone to make some sort of passing grade on their O.W.L. exams, even if they were not intending to try for his N.E.W.T. class. Anyone who made a poor grade would deal with his "displeasure".
</p><p>In addition to being strict, he was not always fair. His having been bullied so much as a child may have fuelled his oppressiveness as a teacher. During Harry Potter's years at the school, Snape particularly enjoyed taking points from Harry's House, Gryffindor. He generally favoured the students in his own House, Slytherin, including Draco Malfoy. However, he was still irritated if they did not live up to his expectations and would punish them too. On at least one occasion, he gave Crabbe and Goyle detention because they had failed their O.W.L. exam for Defence Against the Dark Arts. He also had no qualms punishing Merula Snyde for attempting to frame Jacob's sibling despite her being a Slytherin and seems to dislike her for being perhaps the most atrocious liar and blamer among Slytherins. The students of his house generally regarded him with respect and pride, even cheering loudly when he effortlessly defeated Lockhart with one spell. However, becoming the Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher made Snape fairer (if only slightly) as he lowered his standards to allow more students to enter advanced studies, and he taught the lectures with more passion that intrigued his students' interests.
</p><p>Although he disliked most students, a feeling that is quite mutual, he was not truly evil and did felt quite a lot of concern for their safety and well-being. After Rowan Khanna's tragic murder at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</a> rendered the student body devastated and mournful during the <a href="/wiki/1989%E2%80%931990_school_year" title="1989–1990 school year">1989–1990 school year</a>, Snape proceeded to teach his <a href="/wiki/Sixth_year" title="Sixth year">sixth years</a> how to concoct the <a href="/wiki/Potion_for_Dreamless_Sleep" title="Potion for Dreamless Sleep">Dreamless Sleep Potion</a> in <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions class</a>, due in part to many of his students suffering from sleep-deprived nights following Khanna's death. He was also noted to be particularly patient by <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob's sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> during that specific Potions class, sympathising with the grief his class felt and patiently urging them to focus on his lesson.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">[37]</a></sup> In <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, when Professor McGonagall informed the staff that a student had been captured by the monster from the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>, Snape displayed a hint of genuine concern by gripping the back of a chair very hard. He also did everything he could to protect the students from Voldemort's control of Hogwarts, while Alecto and Amycus Carrow were appointed at the school, further showing he did care for his students even if he rarely showed it.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Order_of_the_Phoenix_members">Order of the Phoenix members</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Fred Weasley</b>: "<i>Git.</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>He's on our side now.</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Fred Weasley</b>: "<i>He's still a git.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; Fred and Hermione about Snape's behaviour towards them<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 251px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150206155602" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Order of the Phoenix – first generation"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg" 	data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix – first generation.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20150206155602"  	 width="251"  	 height="102"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20150206155602" 	 alt="Order of the Phoenix – first generation"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg" 	data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix – first generation.jpg" 	 	 width="251"  	 height="102"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The original <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape's relationships with some members of the Order of the Phoenix have already been established: <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a>, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> and <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>.
</p><p>Snape was not particularly gracious towards <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>, probably because she was so close to Remus Lupin. When they met at school in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, he maliciously said "I was interested to see your new Patronus. I think you were better off with the old one... the new one looks weak." Snape did, however, respect Tonks' abilities as he was her Potions master whilst she was a Hogwarts student and she earned an O in her O.W.L. This is evident as he never let one with a lesser grade take the N.E.W.T which was a requirement to be an auror. Tonks was shocked when Snape killed Dumbledore and never learned that Snape was on their side, as she was killed by Bellatrix Lestrange during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
