</p><p>Snape had a mixed relationship with the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a>. While he disliked their children, he seemed to be on civil terms with <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur</a> and <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly</a>. However, when he murdered Dumbledore, the Weasley family obviously turned against him. Snape also accidentally cursed off George's ear, during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, while he was trying to hit another Death Eater. The Weasley family learned that Snape was on their side in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, except Fred, who was killed in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p><p>He also did not much care for a fellow member of the Order <a href="/wiki/Mundungus_Fletcher" title="Mundungus Fletcher">Mundungus Fletcher</a>, who was also a thief. In <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a> he was arrested for impersonating an <a href="/wiki/Inferius" title="Inferius">Inferius</a>. When <a href="/wiki/Seamus_Finnigan" title="Seamus Finnigan">Seamus Finnigan</a> asked Snape about it, he answered that the "Inferius" was, in fact, <i>a smelly sneak thief named Mundungus Fletcher</i>. It is most likely that Mundungus learned that Snape was on their side after the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>.
</p><p>It is likely that the members of the Order who survived the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> were told by Harry of Snape's true loyalties.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Jacob.27s_sibling">Jacob's sibling</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source: Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire"><b>Snape</b>: "<i>I wanted anyone watching to believe that we were at odds...</i>"
</dd><dd><b>Jacob's sibling</b>: "<i>Aren't we <b>always</b> at odds?</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212; Snape and Jacob's sibling<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup>
</dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 220px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Jacob%27s_sibling_generic.png/revision/latest?cb=20200428175803" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jacob&amp;#039;s sibling generic"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jacob%27s_sibling_generic.png" 	data-image-name="Jacob&#39;s sibling generic.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Jacob%27s_sibling_generic.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200428175803"  	 width="220"  	 height="275"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Jacob%27s_sibling_generic.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200428175803" 	 alt="Jacob&amp;#039;s sibling generic"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jacob%27s_sibling_generic.png" 	data-image-name="Jacob&#39;s sibling generic.png" 	 	 width="220"  	 height="275"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jacob%27s_sibling_generic.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob's sibling">Jacob's sibling</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Much like for <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, Snape seemed to harbour a particular dislike for <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob's sibling">Jacob's sibling</a>. He first met the student when they were having a quarrel with the imperious <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> <a href="/wiki/Merula_Snyde" title="Merula Snyde">Merula Snyde</a> outside <a href="/wiki/Potions_classroom" title="Potions classroom" class="mw-redirect">his dungeon</a>, and callously dismissed their reason for arguing with her in defence of their best friend <a href="/wiki/Rowan_Khanna" title="Rowan Khanna">Rowan Khanna</a>. Due to the sordid reputation of <a href="/wiki/Jacob_(Hogwarts_student)" title="Jacob (Hogwarts student)">their brother</a> casting much apprehension over both the staff and student body, Snape was initially mistrustful of them and made no attempt to hide his contempt for Jacob's sibling during their first-ever <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions class</a>. When their potion was egregiously sabotaged by Merula, Snape's disdain for them was exacerbated, with him unfairly deducting 10 <a href="/wiki/House_points" title="House points">House points</a> from them as punishment for their supposed incompetence. He continued to mistreat them even further after their unsanctioned duel with Merula, being largely dismissive of who instigated the fight but unreasonably assuming that Jacob's sibling was the one who started it. His dislike for them was great enough that he unsuccessful appealed to <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> for their immediate expulsion from Hogwarts, and, disregarding the fact that his aforementioned Slytherin student also had her own part to play in the duel, cruelly subtracted an additional 20 House points from Jacob's sibling soon after. 
</p><p>The student in question, however, was always courteous and civil towards Snape, going so far as to openly acknowledge the latter as being an exceptional teacher on the infrequent occasions that he wasn't berating them, with Snape gradually finding himself to begrudgingly acknowledge said student's flair for potion-making. Indeed, Jacob's sibling only ever betrayed signs of impatience or anger whenever Snape became particularly derisive and scornful, with them thus forming a semi-antagonistic relationship with the <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a> over the years. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Patricia_Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</span></h3>
<figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 220px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png/revision/latest?cb=20180827165324" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Patricia Rakepick - Hogwarts Mystery"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png" 	data-image-name="Patricia Rakepick - Hogwarts Mystery.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180827165324"  	 width="220"  	 height="337"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180827165324" 	 alt="Patricia Rakepick - Hogwarts Mystery"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png" 	data-image-name="Patricia Rakepick - Hogwarts Mystery.png" 	 	 width="220"  	 height="337"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Five years his senior at Hogwarts, Severus Snape met Patricia Rakepick for the first time while they were both still students, and took an immediate dislike to her: Bold as brass and with little regards for school rules, and a member of <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor House</a> to boot, Patricia Rakepick was someone whom Severus would one day compare to his arch-rival during his schooldays, <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>, another trouble-making Gryffindor. Whilst it is uncertain what he thought of Rakepick's initial claims about the existence of the fabled Cursed Vaults as a student, he did acknowledge that she was remarkably ambitious for a Gryffindor, and by no means stupid. By the time he had replaced <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a> as the school's <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a>, Rakepick was already a notable curse-breaker and building her career on eliminating her competition. Wary of her true intentions, when Albus Dumbledore invited her back to help break the curses plaging the school and its denizens, their old rivalry immediately reignited, and Snape immediately went about trying to uncover whatever ulterior motives she might have, suspecting that she wanted to use the vaults to take control of Hogwarts.
</p><p>From that moment on, it is known that Snape and Rakepick were engaging in a subtle battle of wits, and even used students to spy on one another. Recognising that Rakepick regarded <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob's sibling">one of the pupils</a> as a potential rival in her quest to find the vaults, and aware how Rakepick dealt with rivals, Snape cleverly had said student serving as his spy to shift her attention over on him to protect the student as a supposed mastermind of the youngster's actions, while also using the ploy as a tool to try and learn what Rakepick was up to and expose her to Dumbledore, the one person whom they knew for a certainty would be able to put a stop to her plot, whatever it might be.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span></h2>
<p><i>Severus</i> means "stern" in <a href="/wiki/Latin" title="Latin">Latin</a>, and is the root of the English word "severe".<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">[38]</a></sup> It was a <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Roman" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Roman">Roman</a> cognomen, common to members of the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Severan_dynasty" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Severan dynasty">Severan dynasty</a> of Emperors, including one notorious for his harsh persecution of the early Christians.
</p><p>Septimius Severus, also known as Severus, was Roman Emperor from 193 to 211. As a young man, he advanced through the customary succession of offices under the reigns of Marcus Aurelius and Commodus. Severus seized power after the death of Emperor Pertinax in 193 during the Year of the Five Emperors. After deposing and killing the incumbent emperor Didius Julianus, Severus fought his rival claimants, the generals Pescennius Niger (possibly <a href="/wiki/Phineas_Nigellus_Black" title="Phineas Nigellus Black">Phineas Nigellus Black</a>) and Clodius Albinus (<a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>). Niger was defeated in 194 at the Battle of Issus in Cilicia. Later that year Severus waged a short punitive campaign beyond the eastern frontier, annexing the Kingdom of Osroene as a new province. Severus defeated Albinus three years later at the Battle of Lugdunum in Gaul.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> has said that she took the surname Snape from an <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">English</a> village<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">[39]</a></sup> in <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Suffolk" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Suffolk">Suffolk</a>. There is also a village called "<i>Snape</i>" in <a href="/wiki/Yorkshire" title="Yorkshire">Yorkshire</a>, which was rebuilt by the aforementioned emperor, <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Septimus_Severus" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Septimus Severus">Septimus Severus</a>. Snape is also an English verb meaning "to be hard upon, rebuke, snub", derived from the Old Norse "<i>sneypa"</i>, "to outrage, dishonour, disgrace".<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">[40]</a></sup>
</p><p>Interestingly J.K. Rowling used to live in Clapham Junction at the time of her starting to write the first book. Opposite Clapham Junction station is a road named Severus Road, though it is unknown if this is simply a coincidence.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Behind_the_scenes">Behind the scenes</span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span>"<i>Well, that is Snape’s tragedy. Given his time over again he would not have become a Death Eater, but like many insecure, vulnerable people (like Wormtail) he craved membership of something big and powerful, something impressive. He wanted Lily and he wanted Mulciber too. He never really understood Lily’s aversion; he was so blinded by his attraction to the dark side he thought she would find him impressive if he became a real Death Eater.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.the-leaky-cauldron.org/2007/7/30/j-k-rowling-web-chat-transcript">2007 Web Chat Transcript</a>
</dd><dd></div>
</dd></dl>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Grudge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111008205813" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Grudge"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Grudge.jpg" 	data-image-name="Grudge.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Grudge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111008205813"  	 width="250"  	 height="205"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Grudge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111008205813" 	 alt="Grudge"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Grudge.jpg" 	data-image-name="Grudge.jpg" 	 	 width="250"  	 height="205"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Grudge.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Mary_GrandPr%C3%A9" title="Mary GrandPré">Mary GrandPré</a> illustrates Snape perusing the Marauder's Map</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/61/JKR_Severus_Snape_illustration.png/revision/latest?cb=20160823205820" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="JKR Severus Snape illustration"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="JKR_Severus_Snape_illustration.png" 	data-image-name="JKR Severus Snape illustration.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/61/JKR_Severus_Snape_illustration.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160823205820"  	 width="180"  	 height="183"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/61/JKR_Severus_Snape_illustration.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160823205820" 	 alt="JKR Severus Snape illustration"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="JKR_Severus_Snape_illustration.png" 	data-image-name="JKR Severus Snape illustration.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="183"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:JKR_Severus_Snape_illustration.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape as illustrated by <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/SnapeWU.png/revision/latest?cb=20200716131635" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="SnapeWU"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="SnapeWU.png" 	data-image-name="SnapeWU.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/SnapeWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200716131635"  	 width="180"  	 height="180"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/SnapeWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200716131635" 	 alt="SnapeWU"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="SnapeWU.png" 	data-image-name="SnapeWU.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="180"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:SnapeWU.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape as he appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Wizards_Unite" title="Harry Potter: Wizards Unite">Harry Potter: Wizards Unite</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Severus Snape is portrayed by the late <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">British</a> actor <a href="/wiki/Alan_Rickman" title="Alan Rickman">Alan Rickman</a> in all of the film adaptations, making him one of the 14 characters to appear in all eight film adaptations. He was Rowling's first choice for the role. Rickman died of cancer on January 14, 2016.
</li><li>It appears that he also played his part very well. Rupert Grint admitted to being afraid of him in an interview.
</li><li>Due to the age difference between Rickman and Snape, as he is portrayed in the book, make-up was used on Rickman to make him look younger.
</li><li>Snape came very close to receiving <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Merlin" title="Order of Merlin">Order of Merlin</a>, First Class for subduing <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i>.
</li><li>Snape's character was loosely inspired by an unpleasant chemistry teacher J.K. Rowling had in secondary school.<sup class="noprint">&#91;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Wikipedia:Citing sources"><i><span title="The material in the vicinity of this tag needs references to reliable sources." style="white-space: nowrap;">citation needed</span></i></a>&#93;</sup>
</li><li>When asked what Snape smelled like, <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> answered: "<i>Bitterness and old shoes.</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-bitternessandoldshoes_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bitternessandoldshoes-40">[41]</a></sup>
</li><li>Rickman had conversations with Rowling about his character and is one of the few Harry Potter actors that she spoke to prior to the completion of the book series about the future direction of the character. "<i>He knew very early on that he'd been in love with Lily</i>," said Rowling. "<i>He needed to understand [...] where this bitterness towards this boy who's the living example of her preference for another man came from.</i>" Rickman used this knowledge of Snape's ultimate loyalties throughout the films by deciding how to play certain scenes, deliver specific lines, or using body language to convey specific emotions. When the directors of the films would ask him why he was doing a scene a certain way or delivering a line in a specific manner, Rickman would simply reply that he knew something they did not.
</li><li>Much like Gilderoy Lockhart, Snape's character is altered to appear more likeable in the films than in the books. He does not openly insult or harass his students, with the exception of shoving or whacking Harry and Ron on the head to make them focus on their studies, and once when Ron sniggered when Umbridge was embarrassing him. He is notably less cruel to Harry than in the books, such as wishing him good luck on his first Quidditch match and even flashing him a slight smile, along with a sarcastic compliment on Harry's defeat of the mountain troll earlier that year.<sup id="cite_ref-PSf_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PSf-41">[42]</a></sup> He initially defended him, Ron, and Hermione in the second film from Filch's accusations when Mrs Norris was petrified, though he did note that there was a set of suspicious circumstances. Additionally, in the final film, when he talks with Dumbledore after revealing the Prophecy to Voldemort, he asks him to protect the entire Potter family, rather than only Lily, without Dumbledore having to prompt him to do so. Snape is also slightly more laid back and less antisocial in the films. An example is when, in the third film, he gestured Harry out of the Shrieking Shack with his head rather than verbally instructing him to leave.
</li></ul>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 220px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/13/Snape_death.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190919104149" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Snape death"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Snape_death.gif" 	data-image-name="Snape death.gif" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/13/Snape_death.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190919104149"  	 width="220"  	 height="92"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/13/Snape_death.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190919104149" 	 alt="Snape death"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Snape_death.gif" 	data-image-name="Snape death.gif" 	 	 width="220"  	 height="92"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape_death.gif" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Severus' death in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>, Snape's death takes place in the school's <a href="/wiki/Boathouse" title="Boathouse">Boathouse</a> rather than the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a>. The art director of the series, Andrew Ackland-Snow, said in an interview with Cine Premier Mexico: "<i>We wanted to change a bit where Snape dies. In the book, he dies in the Shrieking Shack, and we wanted to get him out from, not a conventional interior, but from that kind of box, to do it in a more dramatic atmosphere. We asked [Rowling] if she agreed for that to happen in there and she loved it ... Snape dies in an extremely good way, I gotta say."</i><sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">[43]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9c/Hp082.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100620114616" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Hp082"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Hp082.jpg" 	data-image-name="Hp082.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9c/Hp082.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100620114616"  	 width="180"  	 height="240"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9c/Hp082.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100620114616" 	 alt="Hp082"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Hp082.jpg" 	data-image-name="Hp082.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="240"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hp082.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape as a LEGO minifigure (2007 edition)</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/340px-Snape5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110813151800" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="340px-Snape5"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="340px-Snape5.jpg" 	data-image-name="340px-Snape5.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/340px-Snape5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110813151800"  	 width="180"  	 height="270"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/340px-Snape5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110813151800" 	 alt="340px-Snape5"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="340px-Snape5.jpg" 	data-image-name="340px-Snape5.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="270"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:340px-Snape5.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape as a LEGO minifigure (2010 edition)</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/LEGOSnape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190903221055" href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Snape_Pop.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190506191136" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img 	data-image-key="Snape_Pop.jpg" 	data-image-name="Snape Pop.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="129"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape_Pop.jpg" class="sprite Vinyl">POP! Vinyl</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Despite his status as a Death Eater as well as implications that he had some form of status among them before Voldemort's attack on the Potters, Snape did not seem to be aware of Peter Pettigrew's role in the Death Eaters nor was he aware that Peter was actually the one who betrayed Lily to Voldemort as he seemed sure that Sirius Black was the culprit.
</li><li>It's likely however that he learned the truth following Voldemort's rebirth as he showed much less hostility towards Sirius than before (while still a significant amount) and he was made aware that Peter was alive and on the side of the Death Eaters.  This would likely explain his hostility towards Peter in <i>The</i> <i>Half-Blood Prince.</i>
</li><li>Actor <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tim_Roth" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Tim Roth">Tim Roth</a> was initially offered the role but turned it down to work in <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tim_Burton" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Tim Burton">Tim Burton</a>'s <i>Planet of the Apes</i> (<a href="/wiki/2001" title="2001">2001</a>). Rickman was cast later on.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">[44]</a></sup>
</li><li>According to Rowling, Dumbledore never did anything about Snape's behaviour in class because "<i>Dumbledore believes there are all sorts of lessons in life... and horrible teachers are one of them.</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">[45]</a></sup>
</li><li>In the film adaptations, Severus appears to be rather older than he is in the original books, being in his early thirties at the time of <i>Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</i>. Alan Rickman was fifty-four when he was first cast for the role.
</li><li>In the last film, Steve Kloves added a new scene to Snape's memories in which Snape visits Godric's Hollow shortly after Voldemort's arrival and collapses when he finds Lily's lifeless body among the wreckage in the house.
</li><li><a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a>, when asked if she considers Snape a hero, she said she thinks of him as an extremely flawed anti-hero, stating that though he was quite cold and spiteful and a bit of a bully, he was capable of love and was immensely brave.
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Alec_Hopkins" title="Alec Hopkins">Alec Hopkins</a> plays a young Snape in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">Order of the Phoenix</a></i> and <a href="/wiki/Benedict_Clarke" title="Benedict Clarke">Benedict Clarke</a> plays an even younger Snape in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">[46]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">[47]</a></sup>
</li><li>During one of the sneak missions in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone (video game)">PS1 version</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a></i>, Snape actually says <i>"There is something very special in the Forbidden Corridor that I've had my eye on for some time. We can't let anyone interfere with my plans. Can we, Mr Filch?"</i> as to confuse the player about who is looking for the Stone, although the line ultimately does not make much sense. However, one can interpret it as a way of bullying <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a> into aiding him to protect the Stone from <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirrell</a>.
</li><li>In the books, Snape is one of the youngest teachers to be recruited at Hogwarts school. Having taught at Hogwarts for fourteen years in <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry's fifth year</a>, Snape has been teaching Potions since he was twenty-one (it should be noted that when <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a> applied for the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> post when he was eighteen, <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Armando Dippet</a>, then the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a>, rejected him on the basis that he was too young, although he invited him to reapply in a few years' time).
</li><li>The chapter illustrations by <a href="/wiki/Mary_GrandPr%C3%A9" title="Mary GrandPré">Mary GrandPré</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_States_of_America" title="United States of America">American</a> editions depict Snape with a thin goatee.
</li><li>Snape attended Hogwarts exactly twenty years before Harry Potter.
</li><li>J.K. Rowling stated that Lily Evans may have grown to love Snape romantically if he was not so drawn to the Dark Arts.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">[48]</a></sup>
</li><li>In the book, Nagini kills Snape by sinking her fangs into his neck after being released from her protective bubble. In the film adaptation, Lord Voldemort slashes Snape's throat, then orders Nagini to finish him off. Surprisingly, less blood is shown than in the book. This was likely due to the film's PG-13 rating.
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Phineas_Nigellus_Black" title="Phineas Nigellus Black">Phineas Nigellus Black</a> was cut from the film adaptations of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows</a></i>. Hence, it is unclear how Snape located Harry and Hermione in the <a href="/wiki/Forest_of_Dean" title="Forest of Dean">Forest of Dean</a>. However, in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>, as Neville is leading Harry, Ron, and Hermione in the secret passage Neville states that they "hardly see him," so in that time he could have searched over Britain to find them and give them the sword.
</li><li>Interestingly, Snape is the catalyst for the entire series, since it was he who told Voldemort of the prophecy and begged Voldemort to spare Lily, enabling her to sacrifice her life for Harry, thus enabling the protection that protected Harry for so long and ultimately led to Voldemort's death.
</li><li>Snape is the only Death Eater who could conjure a <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a>.
</li><li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)</a></i>, a scene with Snape was added when Lupin turned into a werewolf: instead of being unconscious as he was in the book, Snape regains his consciousness and goes to look for Harry with the intent of punishing him for his attack on him. When he hears Lupin roaring behind him and turns to find him transformed into a werewolf, Snape proves his great courage by shielding Harry, Ron and Hermione with his own body, taking a vicious slash from Lupin as a result.
</li><li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>, while Harry is facing Voldemort, he calls Snape "Professor Snape". This is the first time that he addresses him with the title other than in his presence which shows that he has forgiven and even come to respect Snape for his courage and his sacrifices. One notable factor of the books was when Harry was speaking about Snape with Dumbledore, the latter would always ask Harry to address him as "Professor Snape".
</li><li>Amongst Severus Snape's possessions that he kept at his home was a curious object called a <a href="/wiki/Dark_Curio" title="Dark Curio">Dark Curio</a>, though the object was only ever named such in the original script for <i>Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">[49]</a></sup>
</li><li>When <a href="/wiki/Jany_Temime" title="Jany Temime">Jany Temime</a> took over the role of costume designer for the films, many of the characters' wardrobes were re-designed, but Snape's costume remained unchanged throughout all eight films, as Temime thought the existing costume, consisting of a black robe, worked well with Snape's character.
</li></ul>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Benedict_Cumberbatch_Snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130211010315" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Benedict Cumberbatch Snape"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Benedict_Cumberbatch_Snape.jpg" 	data-image-name="Benedict Cumberbatch Snape.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Benedict_Cumberbatch_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130211010315"  	 width="180"  	 height="112"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Benedict_Cumberbatch_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130211010315" 	 alt="Benedict Cumberbatch Snape"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Benedict_Cumberbatch_Snape.jpg" 	data-image-name="Benedict Cumberbatch Snape.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="112"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Benedict_Cumberbatch_Snape.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape as shown in <i>The Simpsons</i> episode "Love is a Many-Splintered Thing"</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Snape once made an appearance in an episode of the TV show <i>The Simpsons</i>, in which he was voiced by actor Benedict Cumberbatch.
</li><li>It was because of Snape that Harry Potter became aware and practical of the Disarming Charm (<i>Expelliarmus</i>). Snape used it in the introduction of the Duelling Club while duelling with Gilderoy Lockhart. He said that students should learn to disarm their opponents.
</li><li>Severus and Lily were also close in age. They were born in the same month and year. He was only 21 days older than her.
</li><li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, Chapter 2 (<i>A Peck of Owls</i>), J.K. Rowling includes a bit of misdirection. After Petunia has revealed her knowledge of Dementors, she explains that she "<i>heard -- that awful boy --telling her about them -- years ago.</i>" Both Harry and the reader assume that "that awful boy" is referring to James Potter. However, Snape's memories later reveal that it was a conversation between him and Lily Evans that Petunia overheard, and Snape was, in fact, "that awful boy." This is the first mention in the books of a relationship between Snape and Lily, but the reader has no way of knowing that until later.
</li><li>Snape's actor Alan Rickman died on January 14, 2016 - only five days after what would have been Snape's 56th birthday.
</li><li>Snape's actor Alan Rickman's first and middle initials - <b>Alan Sidney Patrick </b>- spell the word "asp", a type of snake, the emblem of Slytherin. Those initials are also shared with Albus Severus Potter, whose middle name is Harry Potter's tribute to one of the "bravest men he ever knew."
</li><li>Snape and James Potter's respective actors - Alan Rickman and <a href="/wiki/Adrian_Rawlins" title="Adrian Rawlins">Adrian Rawlins</a> - shared the same first and last initials. 
</li><li>A new species of crab has been named after Snape, <i><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harryplax" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Harryplax">Harryplax</a> Severus</i>. The name was chosen because the crab had managed to elude rediscovery for two decades after its initial discovery, like how Snape was able to hide the most important part of the story for years.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">[50]</a></sup>
</li><li>It is unclear why Snape is still alive in the alternate reality where Voldemort won the wizarding war, given that Voldemort should have still killed him as he believed that Snape was the master of the Elder Wand and still desired to become the wand's master.
</li></ul>
